Current Affairs Commentary

The Most Superior Navy Proposal of the United States: Caution 20

The U.S. Senate passed the most superior navy shipbuilding proposal, already approved by the House of Representatives on January 30th, by a majority of 65 votes to 18 on March 7th. This proposal was introduced by Mr. Vinson, chairman of the House Naval Affairs Committee. The shipbuilding program includes one 8-inch gun cruiser, five 6-inch gun cruisers, one 15,200-ton aircraft carrier, 65 destroyers, and 30 submarines. The construction cost is estimated to be between 565 million and 1 billion U.S. dollars. At the same time, it is also planned to add 1,182 aircraft at a cost of 95 million U.S. dollars. The purpose of this proposal is to make the U.S. naval power comply with the limits stipulated in the 1922 Washington Naval Treaty. Such a large expenditure on the construction of naval and air forces, especially when the economic panic has not yet been overcome and international relations are deteriorating, will undoubtedly have a significant impact on all parties.

From the World War to 1928 and 1929, the economic development of the United States was indeed unprecedented. It transformed from a debtor nation to a creditor nation and became the world's leading power. Not only did heavy industry, financial investment, and the chemical industry experience considerable growth, but also the rayon industry, which has the characteristics of light industry, made significant progress. With the expansion of the American industrial power as it is, it is bound to think of ways to protect it. What is the way? On the negative side: First, it must not fear the enemy's blockade. Maintaining the communication channels in the Pacific Ocean is especially urgent. Second, it must be able to cover the transportation of its wartime military supplies and the acquisition of necessities. Third, it must be able to ensure the safety of its territories, including the Philippines, Guam, Hawaii, and Alaska. On the positive side, first, it must rely on bloodless economic struggles as a preparation for armed struggles, thereby demonstrating the strength of the United States and deterring its hypothetical enemy, Japan, from rashly initiating hostilities. Second, it must strengthen its military power as the ultimate weapon to subdue the hypothetical enemy.

Japan has always prided itself on being a maritime kingdom, and its strength should not be underestimated. The United States knows this very well. The most superior shipbuilding proposal passed this time is not only sufficient to seek partial remedies for the domestic industrial sector but also enough to trigger Japan's pursuit and competition, leading it to economic suicide due to excessive military expansion.

However, we must observe the current strength of the U.S. Navy. It is not surprising that the country's leaders are uneasy. Some say that even if the United States moves its entire Atlantic fleet to its forward base in the Pacific—Pearl Harbor—it can only勉力(mianli) maintain the security of the Pacific coast. It is doubtful whether it can absolutely maintain the Panama Canal. The U.S. light cruisers are not as advanced as Japan's new ones, and many of the destroyers are old. The submarine strength is also weak and insufficient to win. In this situation, it is impossible to restrain the activities of the Japanese navy in the Pacific, and it is also a fantasy to restrict the Japanese navy from controlling the power in the Far East. Once war breaks out, the U.S. naval bases in the Far East, such as the Philippines, and the military strongholds, such as Guam, will be ravaged by the Japanese army. Even the Aleutian Islands, which can serve as the vanguard of the U.S. Air Force, will inevitably be attacked and even fall into the hands of the enemy. If the military situation is like this, then how can a certain Far Eastern market not be invaded by others?

Since the United States is aware of the seriousness of the Pacific situation and the danger of its own situation, it has to take the opportunity to consolidate its naval position. Once it has the confidence in its naval strength and is not afraid, it can then further develop the advantages of the air force to control the final victory. If so, then the United States will have the possibility of permanently maintaining its Far Eastern market. Important raw materials can be imported without hindrance, and even the economic struggles that usually carry the smell of military affairs will not be taken advantage of by others.

Disagreement on Silver Proposal Creates Tense Situation in U.S. Congress 21

No Concrete Action Expected Today

President and Treasury Secretary Offer No Specific Opinions

(Washington) According to the common opinion of reporters visiting various members of the House of Representatives, the legislative action regarding silver in this session will depend on the resolution of the House leaders, who will only listen to the instructions of the executive branch. The situation in Congress is becoming increasingly tense today because the House Committee on Coinage, Weights, and Measures has recommended that the report on reconciling the Fox bill and the Strong bill, discussed in Congress on Saturday and Sunday, be handed over to the House Rules Committee for drafting. According to the Associated Press, Representative Scrugham, a leader of the House silver bill, stated that the President will decide what action Congress will take on silver. Representative Scrugham stated that since the relationship between silver and all currencies is so close, this problem can only be solved by incorporating silver into the ordinary currency plan. President Roosevelt and Treasury Secretary Morgenthau have no specific opinions on the silver issue. Therefore, experts believe that the House of Representatives' vote on reconciling the Fox plan and the Taiwanese proposal on Saturday and Sunday is unlikely to result in concrete action. Various factions in Congress have different opinions on the procedure for the silver proposal. The silver purchase bill of Congressman Goldsborough has now been amended, and Mr. Goldsborough has also expressed his agreement. This bill suggests purchasing silver from 50 million to 100 million ounces per month. When silver is 371.22 grams equal to 23.22 grams of gold, then silver purchase should be stopped. It is also learned that the House Rules Committee has not discussed the silver proposal but is prepared to give notarized approval to the plan authorized by the executive branch. Representative Mabee stated that because he lacks reports on the silver issue, he thinks it is best not to overreact to this proposal. It is generally believed that if the executive branch has no intention of acting on the silver proposal, it will use the excuse of preventing the President from issuing an executive order to replace silver purchase with seigniorage to assist the silver problem. (National Telegram, 9th)

Gaining Broad Authority to Negotiate Reciprocal Trade Agreements

(Washington) Today, the U.S. Chamber of Commerce expressed strong opposition to President Roosevelt's request for broad authority to negotiate reciprocal trade agreements with various countries. The Chamber of Commerce stated that the current form of the President's proposal is quite risky. The Chamber of Commerce demands amendments to ensure the protection of American business. At the same time, the Chamber of Commerce solemnly declared that this attitude does not imply any malice towards the President's negotiations with other powers. (National Telegram, 9th)

Japanese Army Burns Down Chinese Eastern Railway Timber Depot 24

Tensions Rise Again Between Japan and Russia

(Moscow) Since the official report from Khabarovsk arrived here today, the diplomatic relations between Japan and Russia have become increasingly tense. This report stated that Japanese troops, while fighting "Chinese bandits" in Manchuria, set fire to the Chinese Eastern Railway timber depot, causing immeasurable losses. Soviet workers tried to put out the fire, but the fire was too intense, and after a long standoff, their efforts were unsuccessful. (National Telegram, 9th)

Telegrams from Khabarovsk and Harbin stated that a Japanese army unit, under the pretext of suppressing bandits, set fire to the housing and offices of the Chinese Eastern Railway timber depot. Although various methods were used to stop the fire at the time, it was ultimately unsuccessful, and the timber depot was not preserved. As a result, several buildings and a large amount of sawn timber were burned. According to preliminary investigations, the losses amounted to tens of thousands of gold rubles. (TASS Telegram, 10th)

Japanese Army Holds Anniversary of the Russo-Japanese War 25

This Day Designated as Army Day

Tokyo Militarized

(Tokyo) The Japanese Army held its 29th Army Day anniversary today, marking the day when the Russo-Japanese War began in Fengtian on March 10th, Meiji 38 (1905). The Emperor attended the ceremony at the Kaikousha Hall, along with Prime Minister Saito, Minister of the Army Hayashi, and other ministers and army officers. General Minami read a congratulatory speech on behalf of the army, after which a banquet began. (Domei Telegram, 10th)

(Tokyo) Today is Army Day. Centered on the army authorities and various organizations, a grand celebration was held in Tokyo, turning Tokyo into a militarized city. At 2:00 PM, the Toyama School military band departed from Kudan Cemetery and began marching towards Sudacho, Nihonbashi, and Ginza, singing "Our Army" and "Battotai March". At 1:30 PM, a ceremony was held at the Yoyogi drill ground to present five patriotic aircraft and six patriotic automobiles. At 3:00 PM, a large-scale joint air and land exercise was held to showcase the elite of modern science. After the exercise, five fighter planes performed high-altitude flights, creating a spectacular scene in the sky over the capital. The Emperor also considered this 29th Army Day celebration to be of the deepest significance. Under the protection of his ministers, he personally visited the site in front of the Yasukuni Shrine, slowly driving the car and paying respects to the heroic spirits who protected the country from the car. Then, he went to the inside of the shrine to meet with the imperial family members and army generals who had arrived earlier. After that, he went to the exhibition site to view the exhibits for a week. At noon, he personally attended the grand banquet, had a simple field meal, and then returned to the interior hall for a short rest. At 12:40 PM, he returned to the palace. (Den-tsu Telegram, 10th)

278 Gallstones Removed from Human Body 31

A Great Medical Wonder

Kanazawa Ms. Yoshiko Noda from Kanazawa City has been suffering from illness for many years. Recently, she could not bear the pain anymore, so she asked Professor Ishikawa of Kanazawa Medical University to examine her. As a result,

She was diagnosed with gallstones. Dr. Ishikawa performed surgery and removed 261 gallstones from the gallbladder and 17 from other parts, totaling 278. They looked like gemstones. After the surgery, the patient's pain disappeared and she is scheduled to leave the hospital soon. Removing so many gallstones from one person's body is unprecedented in the world. The medical community also considers it a great wonder. (Domei News Agency Telegram, 10th)

France Allocates £27 Million to Actively Revamp National Defense

Coastal and Border Defenses to be Completed in One Year, Air Force to be Reorganized to Respond to Emergencies 43

(Paris) Today, the government submitted a proposal to the House of Representatives, requesting a huge sum of £27,000,000 for the construction of national defense. According to this plan, the Minister of the Army will be able to complete border defenses with £14,000,000 in 1934-1935. The Minister of the Navy will be able to build oil stations and coastal defenses with £1,560,000. £11,625,000 will be allocated to the Aviation Department to improve the Air Force based on the principle of quality over quantity, and a first-line aviation team will be reorganized to respond to any emergencies at any time. (Reuters Telegram, 9th)

(Paris) In order for the Army, Navy, and Air Force to implement military organizations or reform military affairs, the government has submitted a draft law proposing (1) to establish special accounting for the Army, Navy, and Air Force, which will be included in the special items of the national treasury; (2) to allow the Army, Navy, and Air Force to spend the following expenses, namely (A) The Ministry of the Army will spend 1,175,000,000 francs in the 1934-1935 budget to complete the northern border defense project; (B) The Ministry of the Navy will spend 825,000,000 francs in the 1934-1935 budget to build liquid fuel storage tanks, deploy coastal defense projects, and enrich aviation, so that it can cooperate with the Navy; (C) The Aviation Department will spend 980,000,000 francs in the 1934 budget to consolidate the Air Force's armaments and various equipment. The purpose is to replace the "quantity" principle with the "quality" principle. The most important thing is to organize the first combat line of the Air Force, so as to be able to respond immediately in case of an emergency. (Havas Telegram, 9th)

(London) It is learned here that the German newspapers are very pleased with the speech of the Belgian Prime Minister Broqueville in the parliament, supporting the principle of German arms equality, especially his discussion of the mistakes of 1919, and his view that it is almost impossible to keep a great power in a state of disarmament forever. Unrest in Spain 48

Internal Strife Brews, Several Places Already in Motion

Government Mobilizes Troops, Public Anxieties Rise

Madrid, Spain is currently still brewing with internal unrest. The Socialist Party's riots and disturbances in several places are causing unease among the people. Barcelona is actively preparing to prevent disturbances. Residents, fearing a revolution, are stockpiling food. The authorities have issued instructions to local prosecutors, stating that anyone plotting revolution against the government, regardless of whether their actions are legal, must be prosecuted. This is the government's first step to suppress the Socialist Party and labor unions. Several provincial civil affairs chiefs have replaced mayors who have failed to maintain public security. The civil affairs chief of Zaragoza Province has threatened to send troublemaking students to the Canary Islands according to law. (Reuters, 10th)

Madrid, today, the Spanish Interior Minister told a Reuters reporter that unrest had occurred in some areas, but generally speaking, the overall situation was still quite satisfactory. Although 100,000 people went on strike today, the day was peaceful. Bakery owners today declared that if a general strike does occur on March 12, they will be responsible for ensuring that there is no shortage of bread, so the worry about a bread shortage during the strike has now been somewhat reduced. Today, members of the Socialist Party in Parliament demanded that all bills unrelated to politics should be passed by an absolute majority, and at the same time, they requested an increase of 1,000 soldiers. Today, it was rumored that 100 national defense troops and 100 cavalrymen were being sent to Huesca, the central location of the 1930 revolution, causing sudden anxiety among the people. Today, about 30 newspapers in Madrid were unable to publish as usual because workers joined the strike. (Reuters, 9th)

The chairman of the Madrid Socialist Youth League was arrested early this morning for unknown reasons. (Havas, 10th)

In Madrid, a group of women and children broke into a bakery, smashed the glass windows, grabbed the bread inside, and shouted, "We want bread!" Also, in the Saint Lawrence area, 150 families, unable to make a living due to unemployment, are boiling grass roots to fill their stomachs. (Havas, 10th)

Greek Parties Reach Consensus on Balkan Pact 49

Government to Issue Declaration

The Athens government had previously promised the parliament to issue a declaration to explain Greece's obligations under the Balkan Entente Pact. However, the opposition and the ruling parties had not reached an agreement on this explanation. All parties may have deemed it hopeless, but yesterday evening, through the mediation of former Prime Minister Alexandros Papanastasiou, the two sides reached an agreement. After unanimous consultation, the government will issue a declaration that uses language that satisfies all political parties. The original text of this declaration has not been notified to the newspapers and will be reserved for on-site publication in the parliament. However, according to general knowledge, this declaration does not violate the spirit and letter of the Balkan Entente Pact, but explains the spirit of each purpose of the pact and the obligations Greece has under the pact. Therefore, some newspapers that have opposed the Balkan Entente Pact in the past have stopped attacking the pact this morning. The newspapers have expressed satisfaction with the government and the opposition reaching a consensus and hope that the government and the opposition can remain consistent. (Havas, 10th)

German Unemployment Decreases 51

Reduced by More Than Three Million People

(Berlin) Since German Chancellor Hitler came to power, he has been working hard to solve the unemployment problem. According to the news released by the government, the number of unemployed people in Germany has now been reduced to the lowest level since 1921. It also stated that the number of unemployed people in February of this year suddenly decreased by 400,000, so the total number of unemployed people has now been reduced to 3.37 million, which is 341,000 lower than the lowest number in the year when Mr. Hitler first joined the government. Based on the above published figures, it can be seen that the rebound in unemployment this winter has not only been offset, but is also very optimistic about the future of this year. Perhaps this year, as a result of the government's efforts, unemployment in Germany can be swept away. Furthermore, the current number of unemployed people has decreased by more than 2.63 million compared with the same month last year, and the most important progress is due to the encouragement of construction projects and the widespread upward development of German industry. (National News Agency, 9th)

Lord Marley Travels to the United States to Give Speeches Against Hitler 52

Building a Jewish Republic in Russia

(London) Lord Marley, the leader of the opposition in the British House of Lords, recently traveled to the United States, traveled 8,000 miles, and gave 80 speeches to plead for the victims of Hitlerism in Germany. He raised 250,000 yuan to build a Jewish republic in Russia to resettle refugees. He returned to London today. Last year, he traveled to Shanghai to participate in the Anti-War Conference. After staying in Shanghai for several weeks, he took a boat to Vladivostok, returned to Europe via Siberia, and visited the Jewish settlements in Russia. He strongly opposes Hitlerism. (Reuters, 9th)

United States Implements Cotton Production Reduction 53

Producing 10.3 Million Bales of Cotton

(Washington) The US government plans to reduce the amount of cotton produced from 1934 to 1935 and has now been able to reduce it to 10 million bales in accordance with the regulations of the London Cotton Association last year. According to personnel from the Cotton Group of the Agricultural Improvement Administration, 15 million mu of cotton fields have been reduced by legal means, so there are only 25 million mu to 27 million mu of land that can be planted this year. It is estimated that the total amount of cotton produced will not exceed 10.3 million bales. The recent proposal by Minkheim will also be implemented, and a tax of 1.2 cents per pound will be added to those outside the 1,000-bale production volume. (National News Agency, 9th)

Anglo-Japanese Cotton Industry Negotiations, Content of British New Proposal 54

Discussing the World Market in Five Regions

(London) The United Kingdom is now seriously trying to break the existing deadlock in the Anglo-Japanese textile industry negotiations. On Thursday, representatives of Lancashire sent a statement to the Japanese representatives containing the final proposal to achieve this goal, advocating dividing the world market into five regions, namely (1) the British Empire, (2) Australia, (3) the Japanese Empire, (4) South America, (5) other countries. Therefore, the United Kingdom and its colonies can be regarded as one region for discussion, which is carried out in parallel with discussions in other regions. The special committee studying Japanese competition has today approved the actions of the British representatives, and the meeting will resume on March 14. (Reuters, 9th)

Osaka, the Japan Spinners' Association received a memorandum from the British representatives and a telegram regarding the policy of requesting a sixth consultation from the delegation stationed in the United Kingdom on the 9th. The members of the association held a secret meeting at 2:00 p.m. to consult. As a result, it was decided to hold a special committee for Anglo-Japanese consultation on the 10th or 12th to discuss the contents of the British memorandum. The contents are as follows:

1. The state of trade between countries is quite cold due to the world's depression. British trade is no exception to this, but only Japanese goods are developing in the world market. Japan should take the same steps as other countries to implement the principle of coexistence and co-prosperity in practice. For this purpose, Japan needs to implement appropriate measures to control its exports.

2. The United Kingdom advocates that Britain and Japan discuss the world market issue.

3. The agreed year should be 1931, when world trade was maintained at a normal state, as the standard.

4. Britain and Japan shall agree on the export ratio of each country according to the ratio principle.

Because the British memorandum has no concessions in substance, the Japanese side believes that there is no room for consideration and has decided to adopt the established policy. (United Press, 10th)

Daladier Defends Former French Interior Minister 55

Never Conspired to Rebel

(Paris) Former Prime Minister Daladier told the Stavisky case investigation committee today that former Interior Minister Frot never had the problem of conspiring to rebel. Former Police Chief Chiappe once told him that Frot intended to form his own cabinet, but this was a legitimate attempt and nothing more. He had never heard of Chiappe and Frot taking any action beyond the political or parliamentary sphere. He did not see any evidence of Chiappe's malpractice in the Stavisky documents, but he felt that Chiappe, as police chief, was too inactive, because he should have approved the arrest of Stavisky in 1931 or at the latest in 1932. Therefore, he decided to replace the police chief. As for Chiappe's claim that someone asked a wealthy cabinet member to provide money so that the Red Army could purchase weapons, he could not remember whether Chiappe had told him about it. (Reuters, 10th)

American Enthusiasm for Supporting the League of Nations 57

Donating Funds to Promote Peace Work

A Wealthy American Woman Donates a Huge Amount of Property

(Geneva) The Associated Press learned that a wealthy woman from Philadelphia, USA, today designated the League of Nations as the heir to her huge amount of property. This is the first time that the League of Nations has accepted private property. This woman is still alive, so the League of Nations refused to announce her surname, but it is said that the total amount of property is very large. The will states that after the woman's death, this property will first be managed by her husband, and after his death, it will be handed over to her sister, and finally to the League of Nations. Before accepting the title of heir, the League of Nations sought legal advice on the matter. According to experts, the League of Nations' financial regulations do not prohibit the League of Nations from accepting property given by a will. The League of Nations authorities stated that accepting the American woman's gift may lead to greater donations. In the future, the League of Nations will have extensive industries in various parts of the world, and the League of Nations' technical and social work will be further developed due to sufficient inheritance. In the past, the League of Nations' political work was funded by its member states. American people have been enthusiastic about public welfare and have funded the League of Nations' technical and scientific research work. The Rockefeller Foundation donated US$66,000,000, in addition to building a League of Nations building worth US$5,000,000, and built a League of Nations library. The League of Nations' health work has also benefited greatly from the Rockefeller Foundation. In short, most of the League of Nations' social welfare work is funded by the Hague Foundation. Rockefeller also donated US$100,000 to the League of Nations to study methods to prevent commercial and private income from paying heavy taxes. Regarding this point, an international draft has been submitted to various governments. The Wilson Foundation also donated 25,000 yuan to build a bronze gate for the League of Nations Assembly Hall. The League of Nations Assembly Hall is the largest in the world and is expected to be completed next year. In addition, there are many donations from American public groups, including a donation of 10,000 yuan from an anonymous person to fund research on reforming the calendar. Another group calling itself American citizens donated US$10,000 for disaster relief in Albania. Donations to the League of Nations around the world are increasing year by year, ranging from a few pennies to several yuan. Children in British primary schools often save their candy money to fund the League of Nations' peace work. The League of Nations has to take simple acceptance procedures for this kind of small donation. In the past, all donations had to be approved by the League of Nations Administrative Council, but now the Secretary-General of the League of Nations is authorized to accept gifts of less than 5,000 Swiss francs that comply with the League of Nations' financial regulations. (National News Agency, 10th)
