Recent Activities of the Northeast Anti-Japanese Volunteer Army

Wang Delin and Kong Xianwu Retreat to the Jilin Border

Chen Dongshan Advances to the Vicinity of Mishan

Harbin Correspondence: The Northeast Anti-Japanese Volunteer Army has recently, due to Pu Yi's usurpation and proclamation as emperor, willingly subjecting himself to enemy control, risen up spontaneously and issued denunciations. Although their advances and retreats cannot fully follow planned implementations, they have given the enemy and traitors a considerable shock. Among the armies that are most active are Chen Dongshan and Gao Yushan in the Hulin-Raohe area; Wang Delin and Kong Xianwu in the Dongning-Ning'an area; Li Jiujiang on the Haisui Railway line; Zhang Yuting on the Harbin-Manzhouli line; and Zhang Kuiwu on the Tao'an-Ang'angxi line. Among them, Wang Delin, Kong Xianwu, and their units, due to the combined advances of the Japanese 10th Division Regiment, the Hirose Unit, the pseudo-Jilin 7th Brigade, Bai Wenqing, and the pseudo-mountainous guerilla force led by Zhang Zikai, retreated to the Chinese-Russian border at Sanchakou for temporary refuge. Wang Delin and a portion of his troops moved to the activities along the TianTu line. On the 27th of last month, in response to a secret agreement with Chen Dongshan's Volunteer Army in Hulin, they advanced to Dongjingcheng to contain the Japanese army and echoed Chen's Volunteer Army. Later, due to a lack of ammunition, they retreated in two parts to various places along the border. Currently, they are contacting Korean patriots from Yanji, Hunchun, and Wangqing Counties, taking a liaison formation, allowing for rest and reorganization before carrying out further activities. Li Jiujiang's unit still has more than 5,000 men, appearing and disappearing between Hailun, Suihua, Qinggang, and Anda Counties, and maintaining contact with Zhang Kuiwu's unit in Zhaodong. One attacks while the other advances, so that the Japanese and puppet troops cannot take care of both ends. Zhang Kuiwu was Ma Zhanshan's bodyguard captain, from greenwoods origins. He leads more than 2,000 men, and is very active in Zhaodong, Dalian, Jiangqiao, Daxing and other places. A month ago, the Japanese army, together with the puppet Wang Shudong army, besieged them. After a day of fierce fighting, Zhang was able to lead his troops to break through the encirclement and retreat to Jingsheng to reorganize. Recently, he has replenished his army, but he feels the lack of ammunition, and it is not easy to advance for a while. Zhang Yuting's unit was the brave general of Su Bingwen's unit in the Harbin-Manzhouli line battle. At Fularji, with a brigade of troops, he resisted the Japanese army for a month. Although the soldiers' hands and feet were cracked by frostbite, they were still able to follow orders and kill the enemy. After Su Bingwen retreated to Russia, Zhang led his troops to continue to resist the Japanese. For two months, the derailment of the train at the Xiaohaizi station on the Harbin-Manzhouli line, and the overturning of the Japanese soldiers' car at the Nianzishan station, were all done by Zhang's army. At the end of last month, due to the Japanese 14th Division regiment, the Hata Unit, and the pseudo-Heilongjiang army Feng Guangyou Unit attacking in concert, the numerical advantage was in the enemy's favour, and the damage was slightly significant. They have retreated to the vicinity of Nenjiang for replenishment, and it will be difficult to have effective activities within a short time. Chen Dongshan and Gao Yushan's two units, with approximately 20,000 men, are led by Chen as the commander-in-chief and Gao as the deputy commander, relying on the Russian border and the dangerous mountains of Hulin to fight against the enemy. They have fought for several years, and the Japanese and puppet armies can do nothing about it. On the 28th of last month, Chen Dongshan personally led 6,000 men to attack Hulin County City. The garrison in the city included a regiment of the 4th Cavalry Detachment of the pseudo-Jilin Army, a large detachment of the Japanese Army, and the pseudo-Army, all of whom were commanded by the Japanese. After a day and night of fierce fighting, more than 100 Japanese soldiers were annihilated, and one battalion of the pseudo-Army was annihilated. The Japanese commander, Mogi, was injured in more than a dozen places, his leg was broken and he was unable to walk. Fearing being captured by the Volunteer Army, he committed suicide by disembowelment. Many Japanese and puppet soldiers who failed to escape were captured by the Volunteer Army. A lot of guns and bullets were also seized. This was the only major victory for the Volunteer Army in several months. Chen's army has now passed Heizuizi and is advancing towards Mishan. Only because the food for the people in the Hulin-Raohe area is lacking, and the Volunteer Army's supplies are insufficient, and clothing is also lacking, so activities cannot be carried out as desired. Chen Dongshan was a commander under Li Du. During the Sino-Russian conflict, he participated in the Battle of Sanjiangkou. After the September 18th Incident, when Li Du's army entered Harbin, Chen's unit was expanded into a brigade. Later, he followed Li Du to fight in various places along the Jilin border. After Li returned to China, a part of his army was commanded by Chen, and expanded its strength, and worked with Gao Yushan to resist the Japanese. He remained unyielding and was always considered by the Japanese army to be a strong enemy. At the moment, the Japanese army plans to transfer the Nakamura regiment of the 10th Division regiment, to contact the 4th Detachment of the pseudo-Jilin Army, and Yu Chen 部, the pseudo-Garrison Commander of the Yilan area, to attack together, in an attempt to eliminate them, but it has not yet been mobilized. (7th)

Chairman Chiang on Propriety, Music, and Time 98

The Central Guidelines of the New Life Movement

Words of Instruction from the Memorial Week at the Generalissimo's Headquarters

Nanchang Dispatch: The Generalissimo's Headquarters held an expanded memorial week on the 5th. Chairman Chiang attended and gave instructions, titled "The New Life Movement Should Pay Attention to Propriety, Music, and Time." The original words have been organized as follows:

Recently, the entire society of Nanchang has been improving day by day, and the soldiers fighting bandits at the front have also been improving day by day. This is a good phenomenon since the launch of the New Life Movement. Today, I want to talk to you about the most important things that the New Life Movement should pay attention to. Last time, I talked about the essence of the New Life Movement, and I have already said that the New Life Movement is to make all our lives conform to the principles of propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame. Because whether it is a country, a society, an organization, a family, or even every individual, to develop upward and to succeed in any undertaking, big or small, they must be based on the spirit of propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame. Therefore, not only the life of the entire nation and the major affairs of the country must be based on propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame, but also personal private life cannot be separated from propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame. This is the central guideline of our New Life Movement. Now let us ask which of these four virtues is the most important. We can know by looking at the order in which these four characters are arranged.

The most important thing is "propriety." Looking back at the subjects taught in China in the past, namely propriety, music, archery, charioteering, writing, and arithmetic, the six arts, "propriety" was also the first. Since "propriety" is the most important of the four dimensions and the six arts, if we want to create a civilized, progressive, secure, and developing country, society, family, or organization, we must first have "propriety." Whether it is the army, students, children, or citizens, if they do not pay attention to propriety, then everything is useless. If those of us who have the responsibility of teaching understand this principle, then there is no one who cannot be taught well. If those who receive instruction understand this principle, then no matter what knowledge they can learn well, and no matter what things they can accomplish. The general problem now is that people do not know the importance of "propriety," so whether it is schools, armies, or society, none of them can become a cohesive whole. If things continue like this, how can we achieve great success, establish great undertakings, complete the revolution, and realize the principles of the Premier?

Everyone must understand, what is the fundamental difference between humans and animals? Many animals can also speak and have various special skills and keen senses. As for diet and living, there is no need to say more, there is no fundamental difference between them and humans. Then, where is the fundamental difference between humans and animals? It lies in whether or not they know propriety. Since humans are human because they know propriety, then if a person does not know propriety, does not value propriety, and does not practice propriety, then he cannot be called a person, and is the same as an animal. Therefore, since our parents gave birth to us to be a person, we must learn propriety, know propriety, and practice propriety in order to live up to our birth and not be ashamed of being a person. Everyone should know that the first book written by the Premier in his life was "Fundamentals of National Rights," which discussed the organization of social groups and the rules of meetings, all of which are basic rules for group activities or public life. The Premier talked about the Three Principles of the People for decades, why did he not write a book on the Three Principles of the People first, but instead wrote "Fundamentals of National Rights" first? It was because he saw that the Chinese people did not understand the order of group life and did not understand etiquette, so he first wrote this "Fundamentals of National Rights" to teach the general public the basics of all etiquette in society. "Fundamentals of National Rights" contains all the spirit of "propriety" and is truly the most perfect and practical practice of "propriety." If people do not even know "Fundamentals of National Rights," then all group activities will be without etiquette and law, and no social group organization can succeed, not to mention the country. Therefore, if we want to realize the Doctrine, complete the revolution, and establish a free and equal country, we must first have a foundation for social construction, that is, we must be familiar with and do "Fundamentals of National Rights" and be able to value propriety, learn propriety, and practice propriety. If every Chinese person can know "Fundamentals of National Rights" and understand the spirit of "Fundamentals of National Rights" and apply it to general affairs, I believe that the revolution would have been completed long ago and the country would have been built long ago.

Why were Turkey, Italy, and Germany able to quickly complete the revolution and build new countries, while our revolution has failed to this day? The most fundamental reason is that no national citizen does not respect social order, strictly abide by group discipline, and extend this to loyalty to the country and the nation, fulfilling the responsibilities of a citizen, and everything can conform to propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame. Therefore, not only will their domestic enemies naturally surrender, but also all foreigners will be awed by this situation. The New Life Movement that we are now promoting is a basic revolutionary movement to build the country and revive the nation. All comrades who participate in this movement, especially leaders from all sectors of the party, government, military, academia, and police, should understand that "propriety" is the most central and urgent thing in the New Life Movement. Whether it is during meetings or speeches, they must always teach them to value propriety, know propriety, and practice propriety at all times. For example, when attending a meeting, one should know how to perform the three bows. Whenever and wherever one hears the national anthem or sees the national flag being raised or lowered, one should show respect. These are the courtesies that the general public must understand, and we must pay special attention to teaching the general public.

There is another point that everyone should know, that is, so-called "propriety" must have moderation. Without moderation, it cannot be called propriety. What is moderation? It is the most reasonable rule and degree. Without rules and moderation, it is chaos and cannot be called "propriety." Therefore, propriety and moderation are inseparable. The meaning of "moderation" is in propriety, and the expression of propriety is in moderation. If there is propriety without moderation, it is the same as without propriety. For example, now a subordinate in the army salutes his superior, but he puts his hand down before the person receiving the salute has finished returning the salute. This is without moderation, not propriety. It cannot be called a subordinate saluting his superior, it can only be considered a superior saluting his subordinate. Is there still propriety in this? It must be known that the person saluting must wait until the person receiving the salute sees you and finishes returning the salute before respectfully putting down his hand. Have you taught these things to your subordinates or students? Not only have you not taught them, but even after I have said it several times, you still do not know how to do it. Therefore, it can be seen how difficult it is to know propriety. Not to mention that the general public in society cannot understand propriety, even this leading organization of the Generalissimo's Headquarters still has things that have not been done well. For example, the master of ceremonies today is not correct. He only knows propriety but does not know moderation. When everyone is bowing and has not yet stood up, he calls for the second bow. When the second bow has not yet been completed, he calls for the third bow. This is without moderation and cannot be called propriety.

Also, the commands shouted in ordinary units are the same. Often, after the first command, for example, "attention," is shouted, he does not see if the people receiving the command have all stood at attention, and then immediately issues the second command, "left face" or "right face." This is also without moderation. It is not known that after we issue a command, we must use both eyes to see all the people receiving the command, and we must wait until each and every one of them has done well according to the first command before we can issue the second command. In this way, the actions can be real and the moderation can be unhurried, and this can be considered propriety. Teaching subordinates or students in this way can be effective. Foreign education is like this, everything is down-to-earth, follows the rules, and comes step by step.

Page 11

Everything is done one by one. The reason why the Chinese army cannot be trained well and has no spirit is because the person teaching only shouts commands and does not pay attention to the person receiving the command, that is, the mouth arrives but the eyes do not. The reason why foreign armies are trained well and have spirit is because their training is real in everything. After a command is shouted, no matter how many thousands or hundreds of subordinates there are, they must see that

everyone has done well before issuing the second command. These words are saying that propriety must have moderation, and we must perform propriety with moderation.

Precisely because propriety must have moderation, propriety and music have an inseparable relationship. What is music? Music is moderation. Only when the moderation is harmonious can it become musical and beautiful, and the rhythm of music and the moderation of ceremonies are really the same thing in terms of meaning and function. Therefore, if we want to know propriety, we must know music. How is our music now? For example, when our Chinese ships pass by places where foreign ships are docked, they play our national music, which is so solemn and majestic and surpasses the general military music of our country. Take the military music of the Generalissimo's Headquarters and compare it with the military music of the National Government or the Military Academy in Nanjing. Playing the party song is the same tune, and the same copper drums and horns are used, but the sound that is blown is much different. What is the reason for this? It is because the people who are blowing only care about blowing and think that it is done, and do not study how to blow it more harmoniously, solemnly, and majestically. In the future, we must pay attention to studying and improving it.

This is talking about the people who play music.

Let's talk about the people who sing. Originally, when we sing, on one

hand, we must watch the gestures of the music team, and on the other hand, we must look at the music, and sing along with the gestures and the music, so that the whole field can be consistent and the rhythm can be accurate. However, when the general Chinese sing, the musicians only care about blowing there, and the singers sing separately here. As a result, they do not care whether the singing is neat or not, and whether the pitch and rhythm are correct. How can this be called music? These are just two extremely crude and superficial things to illustrate that the Chinese do not value music, and therefore cannot know propriety through knowing music, and cannot value music through valuing propriety.

From now on, those of us who are doing the New Life Movement must think of various methods and teach the general public at all times, so that they pay attention to both propriety and music at the same time. The New Life Movement that we are doing, in terms of its method and content, is completely a kind of social education. The purpose is to enable everyone in society to understand propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame, to be responsible, to abide by discipline, and to be able to learn the six arts of propriety, music, archery, charioteering, writing, and arithmetic, especially the two most important things, "propriety" and "music." These four dimensions and six arts are the virtues and intelligence that a person must possess. To be a complete and noble citizen, one must have everything.

Now the general Chinese people think that everything is very good about themselves, and that foreigners are deliberately oppressing us. I think this view is wrong in many ways. It must be known that things must rot first before insects are born, people must insult themselves first before others insult them, and the country must attack itself first before others attack it. It is not known that many things are because we Chinese are too uncompetitive. The virtues and intelligence of the general public are inferior to others. In being a person, especially in being a modern citizen, the various conditions are not as complete as others, that is, they cannot be equal to others. Now we want to promote the New Life, which is to enable the general public to know this principle, realize themselves, be ambitious, and take propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame as the highest criterion, starting from their own daily life, clothing, food, housing, and transportation, and strive to improve their entire lives, and increase the virtue and intelligence of their lives. Not only must they be able to have a personality that is completely equal to the citizens of modern countries, but also they must be able to promote the inherent virtues of our nation, and be able to surpass the citizens of any modern country. Only in this way can they be worthy of being citizens of the Republic of China and filial sons of their parents, and only in this way can they be worthy of being followers of the Three Principles of the People.

Finally, there is one more point that we should pay special attention to when promoting the New Life Movement and teach the general public in society by setting an example, that is, to cherish time. The first important thing is to be punctual. Originally, everything in the universe and life is in the longitudinal and horizontal coordination of evolution, time, and space. However, in terms of the constancy of space and the brevity of life, time is like a fleeting moment, difficult to obtain and easy to lose, and it is indeed the mother of all our careers and lives. For example, in terms of war, I have often said that fighting is fighting for time. Whoever can cherish time and be faster than the enemy in everything can win the final victory. The key to success or failure and life or death is entirely in time. From human life to all life phenomena, they are all based on the keynote of "struggle for survival" and are contained in the vast war, and time determines their life, death, success, or failure. From this point, we can even more clearly see the preciousness of time.

Now the general Chinese people do not know this most important principle, so they do not know how to cherish time and cannot be punctual in everything. As a result, everyone wastes their precious lives, and the entire society and country

and the nation will not be able to make progress or be built up well. Therefore, our nation is regarded as barbaric and backward and is wantonly invaded. Now we are promoting the New Life Movement, and we must enable the general public to understand the preciousness of time, and everyone can strive to be timely and punctual. From the personal daily life to the activities of most people's social groups, they must strictly abide by time and do a certain job. In this way, time will not be wasted and things can be done well. For example, if we have a place and set a time to arrive, we must arrive at that time. These good habits completely depend on those of us who promote the New Life Movement, especially leaders from all sectors of the party, government, military, and police, to be able to set an example and do what they say, and then supervise their subordinates or students to do it, and then teach the general public in society to do it. I have heard that there are very few responsible leaders in the Generalissimo's Headquarters who cannot strictly supervise their subordinates. Every day when they come to work, they let them casually sign in or leave after they arrive. If this is the case, then how can they succeed? How can a military organization be called the highest headquarters? Therefore, I hope that all comrades in the Generalissimo's Headquarters can pay attention to this point, and with the meaning of "advancing to think of loyalty and retreating to think of making up for the past," "correct it if you have it, and encourage yourself if you don't." We must always be the first to be punctual ourselves, so that we can move the whole of Nanchang, the whole of Jiangxi, and even the whole of China. Therefore, we must encourage each other with this. Whoever can cherish time and be punctual is a revolutionary comrade who can achieve great success and establish great undertakings. Whoever cannot cherish time and be punctual is abandoning himself. No matter how good his skills are, no matter how big or small the undertaking is, he will not succeed. Time is the mother of all undertakings and life. If we want to succeed in all undertakings and realize the highest

meaning and value of life, we must first cherish time, and cherish time must start with being punctual.

Today, we are talking about the principles of propriety, music, and time that we should pay special attention to when promoting the New Life. These principles are what everyone should understand, practice throughout their lives, and benefit from throughout their lives. I hope that everyone will do it when the time comes, otherwise they will be willing to be inferior people and take the path of failure. If they can do it, they will be worthy of being citizens of a modern civilized country, and everything can be successful." (March 9)

Chiang Ting-wen Returns to Fujian to Deploy Military Affairs 99

Two Routes of Central Army Advance Towards Northern Fujian

Military Liaison Between Fujian and Guangdong Has Been Agreed Upon

Shantou Dispatch: After Chiang Ting-wen met with Chen Jitang, a concrete plan has been agreed upon regarding the joint suppression of Jiangxi bandits. Therefore, he left Guangzhou on the 3rd at noon and returned to Fujian. At 4:30 PM, he returned to Xiamen. The next day, he went to Zhangzhou to establish the Eastern Route Army Bandit Suppression Headquarters. The Central Army in Fujian was divided into two routes to advance towards northern Fujian. Wei Lihuang was formed into two columns to cooperate with Gu Zhutong and Chen Cheng's two units on the Jiangxi border. Liu Heding was appointed as the commander-in-chief of the Ninth Column, concurrently in charge of Lu Xingbang, Zhou Zhiqun, and Zhang Luanji's three divisions. Tang Enbo was appointed as the commander-in-chief of the Tenth Column, concurrently in charge of Leng Xin, Fan Songfu, and Sun Yuanliang's three divisions. Liu was in charge of the right wing, and Tang was in charge of the left wing. The left-wing army crossed Shunchang from Yanping on the 25th of last month and attacked the bandits from Jiangle. The right-wing army captured Sha County on the same day. The bandits retreated towards Yong'an, Qingliu, Guihua, and Ninghua. The bandits entrenched in Qingliu and Liancheng, seeing the arrival of the Central Army, have retreated towards Guangchang and Shicheng on the Jiangxi border. Li Yutang, Li Yannian, Li Mo'an, Song Xilian, Chen Mingren, Liu Kan, Wang Jingjiu, Chen Qixuan, and other divisions were led by Zhuang Dingwen and divided into two columns to advance towards western Fujian. The first step was to reach Longyan. It is expected that the Fujian bandits can be suppressed before the 15th of this month.

After the remnant bandits in Sha County and Yong'an fled, there are still scattered bandits in Luokeng, Gaoqiao North Township. Lu Xingbang and Leng Xin's two divisions are now converging to suppress them. A main force of the bandits is guarding Jiangle and stubbornly resisting Liu Heding, Zhou Zhiqun, and other units. Gui Zhenyuan and Jiang Yan's two brigades are advancing towards Zhengfang and Zengfang and are required to capture Jiangle within a time limit. Tang Enbo was ordered to attack Jianning and Taining to cut off the bandits' escape route to Jiangxi. Song Xilian, Chen Mingren, Wang Jingjiu, and other divisions have arrived in Yong'an to search and suppress the bandits in Gongchuan, Sanyuan, Xikou, and Shaxi. If they can be suppressed, the remnants of Luo Binghui and Zhang Dingcheng in Tinglian will retreat without a fight. Chen Cheng, the commander-in-chief of the First Column stationed in Nanfeng and Lichuan, and Wu Qiwu, Xue Yue, and other armies are now taking advantage of the defeat of the Fujian bandits and their retreat into Jiangxi and have set off for Luofang to intercept the bandits in Guangchang.

The day after Chiang left Guangdong, Chen Jitang convened another meeting of generals in Meihua Village to discuss military affairs of bandit suppression. Those who attended the meeting were Yu Hanmou, Zhang Da, Miao Peinan, Huang Guanzhang, Du Yiqian, Huang Guangrui, Zhang Zhiying, Jiang Xiyuan, and more than a dozen senior officers. It was heard that what was discussed on that day was mostly military liaison between Fujian and Guangdong, and matters such as supply and transportation. Yu Hanmou will return to Dagengling in the near future to direct military affairs. The headquarters also telegraphed Wu Wenjian, the air force stationed in Meixian, to send planes to Changting and Liancheng every day to scout for bandit tracks.

The Guangdong army previously built deep ditches and high walls on the Jiangxi border, and the defense works were extremely strict. It was heard that after the Eastern Route Army of Fujian took over the defense of Longyan, Shanghang, and Yongding, if they launched a general offensive towards Changting, the Guangdong army in Shanghang and Wuping would also attack Huichang Junmenling from Xunwu. At the same time, all armies would jointly encircle and suppress the bandit areas of Ruijin, Yudu, Xingguo, etc., in order to achieve the goal of jointly attacking the Jiangxi bandits. (5th)

Measures for Destroying Counterfeit Currency in Bandit Areas 100

Limited Time for Counties to Collect and Destroy

Confiscation Upon Discovery After Deadline

Hankou Dispatch: The General Headquarters for the Suppression of Bandits in the Three Provinces of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui has recently found that there is a lot of counterfeit currency in the bandit areas. In remote areas, people still hide and collect and privately use them due to their own interests. After inspection by the Hankou Commodity Inspection Bureau, it was found that the counterfeit silver and copper coins have very low content. According to the currency regulations, the price standard for this counterfeit currency cannot be too high, so as to avoid the possibility of unscrupulous people engaging in private minting for profit, which would be contrary to the original intention of eradicating this evil. Therefore, a request was submitted to Chairman Chiang in Nanchang to formulate measures for collecting and destroying the currency and to issue a general order to all provinces in the bandit suppression area to follow. Chairman Chiang, based on the report, believed that the retention of this counterfeit currency among the people is sufficient to endanger the rural economy and should be strictly cracked down on to prevent hidden dangers. However, the act of collecting and destroying is most likely to cause disturbances. At this time, the coerced have just returned, and there is no time to appease them. If their losses are suddenly increased, it is not enough to pacify the rural areas and show fairness. In order to take care of the people in the bandit areas, the "Measures for Collecting and Destroying Counterfeit Paper and Coin Currency in the Bandit Suppression Area" were specially formulated. All counterfeit paper currency must be collected and destroyed within a time limit. The counterfeit silver and copper coins will be priced and exchanged separately according to the currency regulations and the results of the above-mentioned chemical test, after deducting the cost of melting and loss, to avoid further circulation among the people. The main points of the measures are: ㈠ The provincial governments shall issue a general order to the special commissioner's offices and the county governments to widely announce that within one month, the district public offices shall be responsible for collecting all counterfeit paper currency and submitting it to the county government for public burning. ㈡ The silver and copper content of the counterfeit coins is extremely low. Counterfeit silver dollars will be priced at 60% of the face value, and counterfeit copper coins will be priced at 50% of the face value. Within three months, the county government will advance the funds to exchange them. ㈢ After the expiration of the exchange period, each Bao chief shall issue a pledge stating that there are no counterfeit currencies left in the area and report it to the district branch for verification and then report it to the county government for verification. ㈣ After the exchange of counterfeit coins is completed, the county government shall submit the advanced funds and the number of counterfeit coins exchanged to the financial department for verification and allocation of funds for reimbursement. ㈤ The cost of exchanging counterfeit coins shall be advanced by the provincial treasury. After melting, the silver and copper obtained will be sold to offset the cost. ㈥ After the expiration of the burning and exchange period, if any counterfeit paper or copper coins are found in the counties, they will be confiscated and dealt with according to law. The district Bao and Jia chiefs will also be jointly responsible. The order has been issued to the provincial governments on the 8th to comply with. (8th)

Opening of the Eastern Guangdong District Pacification Conference 101

Lin and Li Arrive in Shantou to Inspect Municipal Administration

Shantou Dispatch: Provincial Chairman Lin Yunhai, together with Li Yangjing, a member of the Eastern District Pacification Committee, set off from Guangzhou on the 26th of last month for an eastern tour, passing through Huizhou, Haifeng, Xingning, and Meixian. At 10:00 PM on the 3rd, they arrived in Shantou by special train from Chao'an. On the 4th, the Shantou City Party Department initiated a mass rally of all sectors to welcome Lin and Li. More than 200 representatives of various groups attended the meeting. Yu Zuming, a member of the Party Committee, delivered a welcome speech. Chairman Lin made a brief speech to the welcoming representatives. After the meeting was adjourned at 12:00, a tea party was held in the city hall. Mayor Zhai Zongxin, Chief of Staff Yang Gang, Zhang Ruigui, the commander of the Independent Second Division, Zhang Jingcheng, the deputy commander and member of the Nanshan Reclamation Committee, members of the City Party Department, Li Hua, the highway patrol chief, Zheng Lingxing and Chen Shaowen, standing committee members of the City Chamber of Commerce, were all present. After the tea party, Lin took a car to inspect various agencies in the city.

The Eastern Guangdong District Pacification Conference opened at 9:00 this morning. The county magistrates attending the meeting were Zheng Xingzhen, Li Jieshi, Zhong Yaokun, Zeng Xiren, Xie Henian, Wen Chongyuan, Xin Xingqiao, Zhang Wodong, Deng Tan, Lin Bin, Peng Jingyi, etc. The military officers were Huang Renhuan, Deng Longguang, Li Zhenliang, Huang Yanzhen, Huang Zhiwen, Zeng Youren, Luo Li, the chief of staff of the Eighth Division, Zhang Ruigui, Zhang Jingcheng, the deputy director of the Nanshan Reclamation Committee, Zhang Wentao, the commander of the Independent Third Regiment, Li Hua, the director of the Highway Bureau, members of the Han River Management Committee, directors of the Chao'an and Luofu Forest Farms, and dozens of representatives of county agencies. The first day was a talk session. The proposals were discussed in groups starting the next day, including pacification, agriculture and forestry, highways, education, society, autonomy, finance, special items, etc. The group leaders convened meetings. (5th)

Improvement of Tea and Silk Industries in Anhui Province 102

｜Joint Planning by the Construction and Education Departments｜

Anqing Correspondence: The cooperation plan between the Construction and Education Departments of Anhui Province and the implementation measures, which were previously discussed by the two departments and submitted to the Provincial Government, and then forwarded to the Bandit Suppression Headquarters of the Three Provinces for approval, have now been jointly submitted again to the Provincial Government by the two departments. The report states that tea and silk have always been major export commodities of our country, and Keemun black tea (including Qimen, Zhide, and Fuliang, collectively known as Keemun) is particularly famous worldwide. However, due to adherence to old methods and a lack of improvement, foreigners have rapidly caught up, leading to a sharp decline in sales. The silk industry also suffers from poor quality materials, resulting in sluggish sales abroad. The national economy and people's livelihood are severely affected. At a time when rural areas are bankrupt and all industries are declining, it is imperative to make every effort to improve the inherent natural products of the province, cultivate specialized talents in accordance with local conditions, so that what is learned can be applied, and industry can be revitalized. After repeated consultations between the departments, in accordance with the principle of cooperation between construction and education, it is planned to prepare immediately to add the following two projects starting from the 23rd year of the Republic: ㈠ It is planned to establish a junior vocational school of tea science at the existing Qimen black tea industry improvement farm under the Construction Department. Before starting the school, it is planned to first identify tea science specialists and send them to tea-producing areas such as Japan and India for preliminary investigation, so as to understand the current tea industry production and sales situation in the international market, in order to set improvement standards, start preparations, and, after the school opens, give them important responsibilities and tasks, so that there is no interference and the desired results can be achieved. ㈡ The silk industry in this province has always been centered in the provincial capital. Although the silk production in Qingyang and Guichi is also developed, there is a lack of adequate facilities. It is planned to expand the scale of the existing silk industry improvement farm and the provincial women's vocational school in the provincial capital, based on the previously submitted cooperation plan between the farm and the school, to establish a high and junior level sericulture vocational school, as the center for cultivating sericulture talents in the province. Intensive research and improvement will be conducted on all aspects of mulberry planting, silkworm rearing, seed production, and silk reeling. After graduation, graduates will be assigned to various places to guide the public, thereby opening up sources of profit and revitalizing rural areas. The above facilities will directly improve the province's inherent production, implement the spirit of cooperation between construction and education, and indirectly alleviate the decline of social livelihoods and increase the intangible happiness of the province. It is reported that the Provincial Government has submitted the report for review at the regular meeting. (March 8)

Verdict Announced in Shandong Library Theft Case 103

Secretary Si Zhengmin Sentenced to Five Years

Secretary Zhao Sentenced to Six Months

Jinan Correspondence: The case of the theft of a large number of antiques from the Shandong Provincial Library has been transferred to the court for trial. After several court sessions, the thief Si Zhengmin and his wife Si Zhao were interrogated in detail. The inside story and evidence were completely verified. Today (the 8th) at 5 p.m., the Jinan Local Court formally announced the verdict: Si Zhengmin was sentenced to five years of imprisonment, and Si Zhao was sentenced to six months of imprisonment. The court proceedings and the main text of the judgment are recorded below.

Court Proceedings: Today (the 8th) at 4:43 p.m., the bailiffs brought the Si Zhengmin couple from the detention center. Si wore a blue cotton robe, blue socks, and blue cotton trousers, with a felt hat on his head. Si Zhao wore a sheepskin robe. Si was in good spirits, but Zhao looked worried. At 5:00 p.m., Judge Mei Lin and Clerk Zhang Tingwen took the stand to announce the verdict. The judge asked, "Are you Si Zhengmin?" Si replied, "Yes." (Asked) "How old are you?" (Answered) "Thirty-five years old." (Asked) "Where are you from?" (Answered) "Pingyin County." (Asked) "Where do you live in Jinan?" (Answered) "41 Houjie Street, Tongyuan Bureau." After inquiring about Si Zhao's name, age, place of origin, and address, the judge announced the verdict, stating, "This case has now been adjudicated by this court. Si Zhengmin is sentenced to five years of imprisonment and deprived of public rights for eight years. Si Zhao is sentenced to six months of imprisonment. The number of days detained before the judgment is finalized will be converted at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. If you do not agree with the judgment, you have ten days to appeal. The appellate body is the High Court." Si Zhengmin declared in court that he did not agree, stating that all the antiques were indeed picked up and not stolen. He said that he could not accept such a judgment. He added that his wife did not help with the transportation and should not be found guilty or have her crime added to his sentence, and requested the judge to release his wife in court. The judge said, "Your denial of theft is incorrect, because it was already past 7:00 p.m. at that time. Thieves cannot steal things, linger, and wait for you to pick them up. Although Si Zhao was unable to assist in the theft, she did transport the stolen goods." Then, the judge read out the main text of the judgment and adjourned the court. The Si Zhengmin couple were returned to custody.

Main Text of the Judgment: Main Text of the Si Zhengmin Theft and Stolen Goods Case: Si Zhengmin is sentenced to five years of imprisonment and deprived of public rights for eight years for destroying walls, entering a residence at night, and stealing the property of others. Si Zhao is sentenced to six months of imprisonment for transporting stolen goods. The number of days detained before the judgment is finalized will be converted at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. (March 8)

Songjiang Fellow-Provincials Association in Beijing Requests Repair of the Jiangnan Seawall 104

｜Executive Yuan and National Economic Council Have Approved and Are Reviewing｜

The Jiangnan Seawall spans Songjiang, Baoshan, Taicang, and other counties, and is a guarantee for the lives and property of the people in the three prefectures of Suzhou, Songjiang, and Taizhou. It has been in disrepair for many years, and the danger is alarming. Last winter, the Jiangsu Provincial Government submitted a request to the Executive Yuan and the National Economic Council for planning and handling the repairs, which required 1.2 million yuan in construction funds. However, due to the emptiness of the national treasury, it has not been carried out. Millions of people along the coast are increasingly anxious and are running around calling for help. The Songjiang Fellow-Provincials Association in Beijing, including Niu Yongjian, Wang Guangqi, Zhu Shuyuan, Shen Li, and Xia Guangyu, submitted separate requests to the Executive Yuan and the National Economic Council, requesting the allocation of funds and the start of construction as soon as possible. The requests have been approved and are under review. If construction can start soon, it will benefit the national economy and people's livelihood. The original requests and the approval from the Executive Yuan and the National Economic Council are recorded below.

The Songjiang Fellow-Provincials Association in Beijing submitted a petition stating: "Submitting a petition for the Jiangnan Seawall, which urgently needs repairs, urgently requesting the prompt allocation of funds and the start of construction as soon as possible to protect the people's livelihood and benefit the party and the country. Jiangnan has always been known as a prosperous area, and the seawall is the guarantee of prosperity. If the seawall is not repaired, the sea tide will invade, the embankments will collapse, the fertile land will turn into barren salt flats, and the vitality will never recover. The national economy and the people's livelihood are of great importance.

The Jiangnan Seawall in Jiangsu Province spans Songjiang, Baoshan, Taicang, and other counties. Under the old system of the former Qing Dynasty, special commissioners were appointed to manage it, and national funds were used to carry out the work. Repairs were carried out on time, and there were no collapses. Since the establishment of the Republic of China, the country has been in chaos, and the financial resources of the state and provinces have been exhausted. The important task of seawall construction has been put on hold. Disasters have repeatedly occurred due to floods,

and the losses have been great. Only patching and repairing have been done, and no fundamental repairs have been made. Over time, the foundation of the seawall has become weak and the body of the seawall has sunk, leading to the great calamity of the twentieth year of the Republic. The seawall was severely damaged again by the typhoons of last autumn, with numerous holes and cracks and a crisis lurking everywhere. If it is not fundamentally repaired, how can safety be ensured in the long term? However, the project is huge and funds are scarce, and it is not easy to start. Those who are planning to deal with the disaster are sitting and talking, but have not taken action. The consequences are worrying, and we tremble to think of them. The Jiangsu Provincial Government, seeing this situation, submitted a request to your association in November of last year to plan and handle the repairs. All the people are stretching their necks and standing on tiptoe, waiting for the implementation of the good policies. However, time has passed and the year has been renewed, but we have not heard any announcements of the plan or the allocation of funds. The people's eager expectations have inevitably turned into disappointment. Your association's overall planning and construction is not limited to seawall construction, but seawall construction is the most urgent task. It seems that the most urgent matters should be addressed first to prevent disasters. This is different from other construction projects, which are of a more moderate nature and can be discussed at leisure. The two should not be treated equally. The cost of repairing the seawall in the four counties of Songjiang, Baoshan, and Taicang is 1.2 million yuan. It was originally planned to raise funds and start construction by the end of last year, otherwise it would be impossible to defend against the autumn floods this year, and the situation would be irreversible. The Jiangsu Provincial Government also stated this emphatically in its previous submission to the Executive Yuan. The matter must be done, and time waits for no one. Millions of lives along the coast are living in a leaky boat in the wind and rain, trembling in fear of the approaching waves, their cries shaking the ground, a tragic scene that is unbearable to hear. The members of the association are deeply concerned about their homeland and cannot ignore the situation. If there is any negligence in the seawall project, not only will the foundation of the social economy be shaken, but the source of the country's finances will also be swept away. What we feel is dangerous, and we cannot remain silent. Therefore, we specially submit this petition, hoping that you will appreciate that the Jiangnan Seawall is related to the national economy and the people's livelihood, and promptly raise the necessary funds and start construction as soon as possible to eliminate the major disaster and achieve lasting peace. The people of Suzhou will be fortunate, and the party and the country will be fortunate. Respectfully submitted to the National Economic Council." (The text submitted to the Executive Yuan is largely the same, so it is omitted)

The Executive Yuan approved and stated: "The petition has been received. Regarding the case of repairing the Jiangnan Seawall, we previously sent a letter to the National Economic Council to plan and handle the matter, and received a reply stating that the planning documents of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces had been reviewed and handed over to the Water Conservancy Department of the Council for detailed review and handling, and instructed us to investigate and handle the matter. The Executive Yuan ordered the governments of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces to be informed. The content of the petition has been communicated to the National Economic Council for verification and handling. Please be informed."

The National Economic Council replied in a letter: "Received your letter stating that the Jiangnan Seawall urgently needs repairs and requesting the prompt allocation of funds for construction. Regarding the case of repairing the Jiangnan Seawall, we previously received a letter from the Executive Yuan forwarding the Jiangsu and Zhejiang provincial governments' plans for reorganizing the seawall. The plans have been handed over to the Water Conservancy Department of the Council for review. We have also sent separate letters to the governments of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, requesting them to consider the situation and separately formulate detailed plans, and submit them along with various charts for comprehensive planning. We have received your letter and will handle the matter together with the above-mentioned plans and charts. We hereby reply for your information."

Hankou Headquarters to Pilot State-Run Farms 105

Proclamation to Clear Public and Private Property Rights

Private Sales are Invalid

Hankou Correspondence: Since the construction of the sluice gate at Jinkou, over one million mu of lake wasteland in the contiguous area of ​​Wuchang, Xianning, Puchi, and Jiayu counties has been transformed into fertile land. The Headquarters of the Three Provinces for Bandit Suppression, pursuant to the telegram order from Commander-in-Chief Chiang Kai-shek from Jiangxi, will pilot large-scale state-run farms in the area, directly managed by the Headquarters. Preparations are now actively underway, and it has been decided to first clear up public and private property rights. All private speculative sales after the construction of the sluice gate will be invalid. On the 7th, the Headquarters issued a proclamation, ordering the Hubei Provincial Government to post it in the four counties, so that everyone knows. The command and proclamation are recorded as follows: ㈠ Headquarters command to the Provincial Government: "Regarding the case of using the lake wasteland emerged after the construction of the Jinkou sluice gate for piloting state-run farms, the Jianghan Engineering Bureau was previously instructed to report on all preparatory matters as soon as possible, and the order was noted on file. However, the public and private property rights in the area are extremely confused, and it is necessary to properly sort them out to avoid encroachment. In addition to the Headquarters formulating measures and assigning personnel to investigate and register the property rights, a proclamation is issued to the Provincial Government, which should be promptly forwarded to the county governments of Jiayu, Puchi, Xianning, and Wuchang counties for posting and notification, and strictly comply with the order." ㈡ "Inquiring that the Jinshui River basin in Hubei Province covers Jiayu, Puchi, Xianning, and Wuchang counties, with an area of ​​over one million mu. For years, it has been subject to the backflow of the Yangtze River, and every spring and summer, it has been flooded, causing disasters and unspeakable harm. The Headquarters has consulted with the National Economic Council to allocate large sums of money to build the Jinkou sluice gate, and has instructed the Jianghan Engineering Bureau to design and construct it. After more than a year of work, it has finally been completed, benefiting the residents along the lake. It has been decided to use the emerged lake wasteland to pilot state-run farms. However, the area, once a swamp, has been transformed into fertile land, which may lead to people coveting it, hoping to occupy it, speculate in purchases, and dispute with false contracts. If preventive measures are not taken in advance, it will inevitably lead to disputes, and the national economy and the people's livelihood will suffer. The disputes over public and private property rights in the area should be resolved after the Headquarters sends personnel to conduct a clear investigation and registration. From the date of the construction of the sluice gate last year, all private speculative sales of Jinshui farmland will be invalid to prevent confusion. In addition to ordering the Hubei Provincial Government to comply with the order, this proclamation is issued to the residents of the area, so that they all comply with it, and shall not privately buy and sell Jinshui farmland, lest they regret it later. Proclaimed by Commander-in-Chief Chiang Kai-shek and Deputy Commander Zhang Xueliang." (March 7)

Nanhui: Eighth District Intercepts Kidnapped Victim from Fengxian 106

In the Wangjiagang area of ​​the eighth district of the county, a boat suddenly passed by late at night the other day. Coincidentally, Chen Rongsheng, the chief of the 17th jia in the eighth district, and Shao Housheng, the deputy chief, led a team to patrol and saw the boat, which looked suspicious. They immediately ordered it to stop for inspection. Unexpectedly, the boat was a bandit boat. Three bandits on board jumped into the water and fled. The chief and others chased after them, but because it was dark, they escaped. They only rescued one kidnapped victim and recovered many stolen goods. It is said that his name is Xu Liuying, and he is from the fourth district of Fengxian County. He was kidnapped by more than 30 bandits. However, the kidnapped victim suffered from the cold after entering the water, and his feet were frozen and unable to walk. His family was notified in advance to take him back for treatment. He has now recovered and has been sent to the district for investigation.

Kunshan: Bureau Chief Beaten for Banning Dragon Lantern Festival 107

Recently, ordinary workers outside the east gate of the county initiated a dragon lantern festival, followed by Youfang Temple and the southeast gate. They paraded in the evening until sunset, with dramas interspersed in the dragon lanterns. Tens of thousands of people watched. The county's Public Security Bureau Chief Hua Shijun, fearing that it would disturb the peace, issued a notice to ban it. However, those people turned a deaf ear. At 8 p.m. on the 9th, the dragon lanterns outside the east gate arrived in front of the county government. Coincidentally, Public Security Bureau Chief Hua Shijun came from the south and stepped forward to dissuade them, which angered the crowd. With a shout of "beat him," he was beaten in the waist. Fortunately, he was clever and escaped to the Yuantai Hotel, where he was out of danger. The crowd, seeing that they had caused trouble, gathered several hundred people and crowded into the Malu Sub-Bureau, demanding an explanation from Patrol Officer Dai Younian. Seeing that Dai was not there, they smashed the guardhouse at the entrance and the wooden sign of the sub-bureau and threw them into the river. They also smashed the door lanterns and screens, leaving nothing intact. The place was in an uproar, and there were thousands of spectators. Later, the Detective Team Leader Wang Yunshan came out to mediate. The crowd demanded to continue the dragon lantern festival for three days, otherwise they would not disperse. Seeing that the crowd was growing, Wang, fearing that something unexpected would happen, verbally agreed. They dispersed at 10 p.m.

Suzhou: Burning Grass as a Game Causes a Huge Disaster 108

In Guangfu Dengwei Mountain in Suzhou, the plum blossoms have been in full bloom recently, attracting many tourists. The other day, a certain teenager set fire to the thatch in the grass behind the mountain as a game. Unexpectedly, the southwest wind was very strong that day. In a short time, the fire spread, and the entire mountain was on fire, covering an area of ​​over one hundred mu. All the thatch on the mountain was burned to ashes. The villagers could not extinguish the fire and could only let it burn naturally. As a result, about thousands of dan of thatch were burned, causing considerable losses. However, the teenager who caused the disaster could not be found.

Orphan Runs Away to Join the Army 109

Shen Baoshan's son, Jihua, who lives at No. 15, Fenyayuan Lane, Old Xue, and works as a secretary in the Suzhou Newspaper Guild, is now twenty-one years old. His mother died when he was young, and he was raised by his father with great effort. Jihua is eager to study and has great ambitions. He often says that a man must serve the country. Recently, he failed the entrance examination for the Provincial Middle School. He suddenly left a letter and ran away on the 9th. Before leaving, he told his sister that he was going to Nanjing to join the gendarmerie and serve the country. His father was very distressed because he loved his son.

Dai Ji Retires from the Political Scene in Suzhou 110

Dai Ji, a native of this county and former garrison commander of Shanghai, went to Hong Kong for recuperation after the Fujian Incident was quelled. The central government once sent Dai to reorganize the 19th Route Army, but it was discussed but not carried out. Dai has now returned to Suzhou and does not want to ask about state affairs. He intends to retire from the political scene in Suzhou.

Thirty-Eight Coffins Burned to Ashes 111

In Changfeijia Cemetery in Likou Majing, there were thirty-eight coffins temporarily placed there. The other day, a village woman named Qian Yin went to sweep the tomb and burned paper ingots. Unexpectedly, the fire spread to the rice straw next to the coffins and could not be controlled. All the coffins were burned to ashes. The police district in charge immediately arrested Qian Yin for handling.

Taicang: Thug Rapes Young Girl 112

Yu Er'a, a girl from Tingziqiao outside the east gate of the city, is seventeen years old and has been betrothed to someone. The other day in the afternoon, Er'a went to the city to watch a Huaguxi opera. When she passed the entrance of the Chamber of Commerce, she was forcibly dragged into the

gatehouse by the thug Qian Jinsheng in collusion with the gatekeeper Zhao Zhaofu, and was raped for two nights. Er'a's father, Yu Genfu, was worried because Er'a had not returned for two nights. When the girl managed to escape and told him what had happened, Genfu was furious. He immediately came to the city and turned Qian Jinsheng over to the Public Security Bureau. After a preliminary hearing confirmed the facts, he was handed over to the county court for handling.

Wuxi: Han Dynasty Jade and Gold Bars Discovered in Ancient Tomb 113

In the fifth district of the county, there is a large grave of the Qian family, which covers a vast area. The family descendants have declined, and there is no one to sweep the tombs during the Cold Food Festival and the Autumn Festival. Therefore, it is generally regarded as an ownerless wasteland tomb. Recently, Mr. Jiang and others from the village initiated a plan to level the Qian family's large tomb and build a ball field for the local youth to exercise and study sports, and it is also planned to set up a station there for passengers on the Wuxi-Jiangyin long-distance buses to get on and off. On the 7th, workers were hired to excavate the tomb. When they dug down six or seven feet, they found a stone tablet, which was extremely solid. When the stone tablet was removed, there was a rotten coffin, which was already in disrepair. The bones in the coffin had also disappeared, with only a large red hat button remaining. Further searching through the soil revealed more than ten gold bars weighing more than ten taels each, and one gold ingot weighing about six or seven taels. In addition, there were countless other Han Dynasty jade items. Among them were two concave-shaped jade pieces, which were likely placed on the hands of the deceased when they were placed in the coffin. The items in the tomb are worth millions. Villagers who heard the news rushed to see it, and the road was blocked. Mr. Jiang and others, fearing that the antiques might be lost, decided to work with local people to jointly decide how to handle them in order to avoid loss.

Inauguration Ceremony of the Wuxi-Yixing Highway 114

The Wuxi-Yixing Highway starts from the Yixing bus station on the Beijing-Hangzhou National Highway and ends at the Wuxi railway station on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway, with a total length of 58.0 kilometers. It passes through the prosperous towns of Heqiao, Caoqiao, Xueyanqiao, Meiyuan, and Xishan in Yixing, Wujin and Wuxi counties. The road surface project started on August 26, 1933, and was fully completed on February 5, 1934. Now that the first phase of the road surface project has been completed, the inauguration ceremony was held yesterday (10th). Hundreds of Chinese and foreign guests attended. The inauguration ceremony was held at 1:30 p.m. At 2:00 p.m., Wang Xiyi, the deputy manager of the company, and others invited all the guests to board ten large buses parked at the station, lined up in a single file, and departed one after another. Before long, they arrived at the Meiyuan station. At that time, there were about hundreds of guests visiting. After the representatives in the buses got off, Director Shen of the Construction Department, representing Wu Shilin, performed the ribbon-cutting ceremony at the intersection, and there was a burst of cheers. A test drive was then carried out, with five cars heading for Yixing and five heading for Xueyanqiao to inspect the entire road. Wu Zhihui, Wu Shilin, and others all took the cars directly to Yixing to inspect the entire road. They returned to Wuxi in the evening. The representatives who came to Wuxi to attend the ceremony returned to the various ports of Beijing and Shanghai that night.

Changzhou: Prosecutor Investigates Jailed Prisoner's Hunger Strike 115

Prisoners at the Wuyi First Prison went on a hunger strike on the 6th of this month because of the reduction in their food rations. After Cui Yun-gong, the president of the county court, entered the prison to comfort them, they all resumed eating. Prosecutor Guan Junjie believed that this matter was of great importance. On the morning of the 9th, he personally entered the prison to investigate. He asked in great detail about whether the color of the rice was good or bad and whether the weight of the rice was heavy or light. He also summoned the warden for questioning. However, because the warden was out on business, Prosecutor Guan temporarily summoned nine prisoners and Fang Bingyuan, an employee in the kitchen, to the court for interrogation. However, the main prisoner who led the hunger strike has not yet been identified. On the 10th, it was planned to summon the warden Yu Liansheng to the station for questioning in order to find out the truth.

At around 10:00 a.m. on the 9th, a certain actor at the Tianchan Stage was careless when cooking breakfast and left a fire on the firewood, which spread to the wooden pillars. When the fire broke through the roof, they shouted for help. At that time, the actors were awakened from their dreams and escaped for their lives. The firefighters rushed to rescue the fire, which was extinguished at around 1:00 p.m. The building was completely burned down. The actress Guo Yurong suffered the most losses. The manager of the stage is now planning for the actors' welfare.

Nantong: Measures to Reorganize Land Tax 118

Land tax in Tong County has been plagued with deep-seated problems. On the 9th, the county government convened representatives from various agencies and organizations to hold a meeting on reorganizing the land tax and decided on the following measures: ㈠ All grain collection counters in the county will be merged into ten locations. ㈡ Tax collectors who failed to collect 60% of the tax last year will be dismissed. ㈢ Land with high assessed value and heavy tax burden, which the people are unable to bear, will be investigated and registered by the county's tax collection office within two months and submitted to the provincial government for review and reduction.

Aviation Department Sends Commissioner to Survey Airport 119

Zhao Zhongyi, a commissioner sent by the Aviation Department, arrived in Tong on the 9th and went to the Tangzhahekou area to survey the airport, so that airplanes can land there when crossing the river.

Changshu: Deadline for Reporting Supplementary Grain Tax Increases 120

The housing base area in the county's urban area is estimated to be about 9,000 mu. Since the former Qing Dynasty, the people have not paid

grain tax. Recently, according to inquiries from the provincial government, since there is no grain tax for the base area, the property rights cannot be determined. In order to protect the property rights of the people, a supplementary grain tax increase is implemented. Each

mu will be taxed at four yuan and several jiao. It is estimated that over 300,000 yuan can be collected from the entire city. The county government has now formulated supplementary grain tax increase measures and announced them to the public, with a deadline for compliance and payment by the end of April of this year. If payment is not made by the deadline, an additional 20% will be added within one month, and 40% will be added within two months.

Continuing Arrests in the Donglai Town Robbery Case 121

Donglai Town in the fourth district is a newly emerging market town and is quite wealthy. In late December of last year, it was robbed by more than 50 pirates, causing severe losses. The detective team intensified its investigation and arrested seven or eight people. The detective team in this county has now received a tip-off that wanted criminals are secretly living in Pudong. Team Leader Zhu personally went to the Chenjiaqiao Kiln Factory in Pudong and arrested Zhang Shaoqing and Zhou Si. They were brought to the county on the 8th. After being interrogated by the Public Security Bureau, the bandits confessed in detail the robbery of Donglai, admitting to the robbery. However, Zhou Si firmly denied being a bandit. The Public Security Bureau decided to send them to the county judiciary for review on the afternoon of the 9th.

Hangzhou: Loan for Qiantang River Bridge Secured 122

Finance Director Zhou Junyan returned to Hangzhou last night (9th) at 11:00 p.m. due to his transfer to the position of Military Supplies

Director to handle the handover. When Director Zhou was in Shanghai, he and Construction Director Zeng Yangfu

contacted the Shanghai banking community regarding a loan for the Qiantang River Bridge. According to Zhou's statement to reporters, the contact in Shanghai was successful. The Shanghai banking community has agreed to lend 2 million yuan, of which Xingye Bank will lend 1 million yuan, the Bank of China 400,000 yuan, the Bank of Communications 300,000 yuan, the Siming Bank 200,000 yuan, and the Industrial Bank 100,000 yuan, totaling 2 million yuan. A preliminary agreement has been drafted and will be signed in early June. Construction of the Qiantang River Bridge will begin at that time.

Gaoyou: Patrol Officer Kills Two While Playing with Gun 123

Wang Hengru, a patrol officer of the second group of the water patrol team stationed in Jinkou Town in the twelfth district, led his team to the home of Xie Jinquan, the deputy town chief of Biantang Town, for a feast the other day. The City Chamber of Commerce Requests the Ministry of Finance to Adhere to the Original Country of Origin Marking Implementation Date 124

Extension Expires July 1st

Immediate Implementation Without Further Extension

Yesterday, the Shanghai City Chamber of Commerce submitted a request to the Ministry of Finance, stating:

Regarding the matter of the request: The "Regulations on Country of Origin Marking for Imported Goods" were formulated and promulgated in February of the 22nd year [of the Republic, i.e., 1933], originally scheduled for implementation on August 1st of the same year. Subsequently, in response to requests from foreign merchants, the implementation was extended to January 1st of the 23rd year [1934]. Merchants looked forward eagerly, believing there would be no further changes at the deadline. Unexpectedly, in November of the previous year, a clear order was received from the government, changing the implementation date to July 1st of this year. This regulation, since its promulgation, has been extended twice consecutively, greatly exceeding merchants' expectations. Marking the country of origin on goods by the country of production is a common practice in modern countries. Last year, various economic conferences of nations passed several measures, the main point being that the implementation of this law should avoid differential treatment for various importing countries. The implementation of this regulation in our country does not involve any differential treatment among nations. Therefore, foreign merchants fundamentally have no grounds for opposition. This is the first point. Originally, Article 1 of the regulations stipulated that the marking should be done in clear Chinese characters. This has been changed to allow marking in the language of the country of origin, which is convenient for foreign merchants and could not be more considerate. There should be no further objections. This is the second point. The purpose of implementing this marking is to prevent producers from using improper competitive means to deceive the public, and to protect legitimate merchants from illegal infringement when selling goods. Therefore, legitimate merchants have no reason not to want the implementation of this regulation. Those with ulterior motives are few in number. The government should uphold international justice and protect the interests of the majority of legitimate merchants, both Chinese and foreign. This is the third point. Based on the above three major reasons, a resolution was passed at the 67th regular meeting of our chamber, requesting the government to implement the aforementioned regulations immediately on July 1st of this year, when the extension expires, without further delay. We hereby submit this case to your ministry for review and approval for implementation.

Nine Types of Public Bonds to be Drawn for Principal Repayment This Morning 125

Total Principal Repayment of Silver $5,549,000

24 Treasury Bonds Payable on the 20th, Remaining Payable at the End of the Month

Yesterday at 10:00 AM, the Ministry of Finance held a lottery for the repayment of principal for nine types of public bonds, including Austrian Indemnity-Guaranteed 24 Treasury Bonds, in the grand hall of the Bankers' Association at No. 4 Hong Kong Road. Over 40 representatives from various sectors attended. Presided over by Zheng Lai, Director of the Public Debt Department, 42 lots were drawn, totaling a principal repayment of silver $5,549,000. All winning bond tickets, except for the 24 Treasury Bonds scheduled for payment starting on the 20th of this month, the remaining eight types are scheduled for payment starting on the 31st of this month by the Central, China, and Communications Banks in various locations, along with the accrued interest. Details are recorded as follows:

Representatives from Various Sectors: Those in attendance included Zheng Lai, Director of the Public Debt Department of the Ministry of Finance; Lu Shuping from the Shanghai Municipal Government; Ju Zhijing from the First Special District Court; Guo Ben from the Inspectorate General of Customs; Yuan Lisong from the Shanghai City Chamber of Commerce; Xia Jilin from the Hankou City Chamber of Commerce; Fang Zemin from the Zhongfu Bank; Jin Wenwei from the Yongxiang Bank; Wang Jiaosheng from the Central Trust Company; Luo Tiehang from the Chinese Securities Exchange; (Supervisors) Shen Zaochi from the Auditing Department; Fan Jietang from the National Debt Fund Management Committee; Hu Bijiang and Lin Kanghou from the Bankers' Association; Qian Yuansheng from the Money Trade Association; (Lottery Drawers) Li Tisen from the Central Bank; Zhu Qizhen from the Bank of China; Mao Rui from the Communications Bank; (Administrators) Huang Guoen, Dong Puming, He Xiaojuan, Liang Yaozong; (Recorders) Chen Shaochao, You Dunti, Ji Juncai; (Document Clerks) Huang Qizong, Ling Qixun, Huang Meizhao; (Receptionists) Zheng Yijian, Chen Jian.

Except for the 17th-year Financial Long-Term Public Bonds, which, according to the original regulations, require a repayment of $1,125,000 each time, and the lottery method must use three-digit numbers, the remaining eight types of bonds will still use two-digit numbers for the lottery. I will now briefly report to you the circumstances of each bond: (1) The Austrian Indemnity-Guaranteed 24 Treasury Bonds were issued in the 15th year of the Republic [1926], with a total amount of $2,400,000. This is the seventeenth repayment. One lot drawn will repay $150,000. Principal has already been repaid twelve times. This is the thirteenth repayment. One lot drawn will repay approximately $100,000.
