Sun Ke Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday 126

Talks on Silver Agreement Include Conditions

American Loan Affects Economic Commission

Min Rebellion Attempts are Powerless

Sun Ke, President of the Legislative Yuan, arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning at 7:20 AM on the night train from Nanjing. Our reporter visited him at his residence on Columbia Road yesterday. Sun stated that the Legislative Yuan has published the draft constitution and is publicly soliciting opinions, hoping that all sectors of the country will provide as much criticism as possible. After collecting opinions from all parties, the Legislative Yuan will convene a general meeting to discuss revisions and create a second draft of the constitution.

Silver Agreement: Sun also stated that the Legislative Yuan has approved the Silver Agreement, but with a statement of reservation to avoid being restricted by the agreement. It will be submitted to the National Government for implementation and communicated to various countries by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs before April 1st. This case was initially drafted by the Ministry of Finance based on the advice of its American advisors, with a statement of reservation. However, after careful discussion by the Legislative Yuan, it was deemed insufficient. Therefore, it was resolved to add a condition to the fourth item of the agreement, that is, China has the right to take necessary actions when Chinese industry is at risk, so as not to be restricted or bound by the agreement. As for the future ban on silver exports, there are various practical difficulties. Therefore, an effective method may focus on increasing the export tax on silver.

Cai and Others' Attempts:

Regarding the rumors that the Southwest intends to establish a branch of the Military Affairs Commission, with Chen Jitang as the chairman, Sun stated that this is managed by the military authorities, and he has not heard of it. As for the rumors that the main culprits of the Min Rebellion, Cai Tingkai, Chen Mingshu, etc., are still staying in Hong Kong and are planning something, Sun believes that the embers of the dead fire will be powerless, and he firmly believes that Mr. Hu Zhantang and others will not be utilized by such people.

Economic Commission Progress: Sun stated that the National Economic Commission recently convened several executive meetings. The overall direction remains as originally planned, with no major changes. Regarding the development of the Northwest, it is deemed urgent and cannot be delayed. Dai Jitao and Song Ziwen will go for on-site inspections. Dai and others are expected to depart within two or three weeks. The sluggish sales of American cotton and wheat affect the funding of the entire Economic Commission, making it difficult to implement all future construction plans. Further detailed discussions will be held based on the evolving situation to devise appropriate measures. When the reporter asked if, in case the construction of the Economic Commission and other matters cannot proceed due to lack of funds, whether there are plans to seek loans from other countries, Sun replied that it is indeed possible to seek loans from other countries to fund construction.

Qinzhou and Lianzhou Native Sugar Fined, Sugar Merchants File an Appeal 127

Requesting the Ministry of Finance to Revoke the Customs' Decision

The shipment of native sugar from Qinzhou and Lianzhou to Shanghai was repeatedly detained and fined by the Jianghai Customs last year. Chambers of commerce from various counties in Qinzhou and Lianzhou, as well as sugar merchants, appointed Pang Songhui as their representative to petition the Customs Administration of the Ministry of Finance in Beijing. Details have been previously reported. It is now learned that the Customs Administration's reply rejected the request for the return of fines and supplementary taxes, and made no mention of measures to ensure the safety of future shipments. Relevant sugar firms in Shanghai and sugar merchants from Guangdong Province have expressed their dissatisfaction and unanimously decided to file an appeal to the Ministry of Finance. Pang Songhui, the petition representative, has drafted the appeal and will submit it to Beijing today. The original text is as follows: For the purpose of appealing against the Jianghai Customs' fines on Qinzhou and Lianzhou native sugar, being dissatisfied with the Customs Administration's decision, filing an appeal, requesting the revocation of the original decision, and making a more appropriate decision. The facts, reasons, and objectives of the request are stated as follows: (Facts) From July to September of the 22nd year of the Republic [1933], Qinzhou and Lianzhou sugar merchants Heli, Henghelong, Guangchanghe, Heyi, and others shipped native white sugar from Beihai to Shanghai a total of five times. The exports were all verified by the Beihai Customs as pure native sugar, taxes were paid in accordance with regulations, and clearance documents were issued. However, upon arrival in Shanghai and reporting to the Jianghai Customs for inspection, the goods were completely detained and accused of being mixed with 10% to 20% foreign sugar, resulting in fines totaling 1,560 silver dollars and supplementary taxes of 1,957 silver dollars. Sugar merchants suffered innocent penalties and unbearable losses, leading to suspension of business and transportation, which had a very serious impact. The Beihai City Chamber of Commerce, together with the Hepu County Chamber of Commerce, convened all sugar merchants and resolved to adopt relief measures, appointing Songhui as their representative to petition in Beijing, which has been reported to your ministry. The Customs Administration's reply stated that, according to the Inspector General of Customs' investigation, the sugar was thoroughly inspected by the Jianghai Customs and found to contain unpaid foreign sugar. The merchants mixed unpaid foreign sugar with domestic goods, attempting to evade taxes. The Jianghai Customs imposed penalties in accordance with regulations, and the handling was appropriate. The request from the Beihai City Chamber of Commerce and others to return the fines and supplementary taxes should not be considered. Reading this reply is extremely difficult to accept and should be immediately appealed to your ministry, requesting the original decision to be revoked and a more appropriate decision made. (Reasons) The Jianghai Customs imposed heavy fines based on the accusation that Qinzhou and Lianzhou sugar merchants mixed unpaid foreign sugar with domestic goods, attempting to evade taxes. The appropriateness of the Jianghai Customs' penalties needs to be clarified: (1) Whether the Jianghai Customs' standard for distinguishing foreign sugar from native sugar is reasonable, (2) Whether the Jianghai Customs has proof for distinguishing taxed sugar from untaxed sugar, and (3) Whether the sugar merchants' ability to mix foreign sugar with native sugar can be used as a basis for judgment. The current method of distinguishing foreign sugar from native sugar by the Jianghai Customs, regardless of the place of origin or source, relies solely on the level of optical rotation and the difference in crystallization. Sugar with an optical rotation above 90 degrees and hard crystals is considered foreign sugar, while sugar with an optical rotation below 90 degrees and easily soluble crystals is considered native sugar. This standard violates customs policy and lacks factual basis. Since the increase in taxes on foreign sugar, the domestic sugar industry has developed rapidly. In Qinzhou and Lianzhou, the raw materials for sugar production used to be only large sugarcane and bamboo sugarcane, but in recent years, improved varieties such as "2725" and "2878" sugarcane have been introduced. The sugar production methods used to be only stone pressing, but in recent years, there have been so-called improved local methods and small-scale machine-made methods. Sugarcane production is improving daily. The Jianghai Customs has not paid attention to the progress of the production area and only knows how to use its three-year-old engraved standard, resulting in repeated detention and fines for improved Qinzhou and Lianzhou native sugar, while inferior sugar can be transported without hindrance. Is this inspection standard reasonable? It remains to be seen. According to the current tax system, foreign goods must pay import taxes before entering the mainland. Foreign goods that have already entered the mainland must be lightly taxed. Native goods must be verified for the collection of transit taxes before being released. Goods that have already obtained transit must be pure native goods with light taxes. Customs regulations are strict, and there is no room for fraud. Now, Qinzhou and Lianzhou sugar merchants transport native sugar from Beihai to Shanghai, holding documents verified and taxed by the Beihai Customs, and transport them directly to Shanghai. The documents match the goods, but the Jianghai Customs accuses them of being mixed with untaxed foreign sugar. On what basis is this accusation made? Is the document verified and taxed by the Beihai Customs valid? Is Beihai the mainland? The claim that it is untaxed is even more absurd. The intention is nothing more than because the inspected sugar is of better quality, exceeding its inspection standard of several years ago, it is judged to be mixed with foreign sugar. Since it is foreign sugar, it must be untaxed. Is this logic sufficient to prove that sugar merchants are evading taxes, or is it just giving customs officials a pretext for serious dereliction of duty? It does not need to be argued by the wise. Now that the Customs Administration has made such a reply, it cannot redress the grievances of the sugar merchants, and it will reduce the credibility of the government's customs administration. This is why the petitioners dare not remain silent. As for whether sugar merchants can mix foreign sugar with native sugar, it is the key to judging this case. The subjective understanding and objective facts are separately proved. Qinzhou and Lianzhou are rich in sugarcane and sugar, and the price is lower than any other production area in the country. Sugar products are only shipped out and rarely imported. Foreign sugar is heavily taxed and burdened with donations, and the freight is extremely high, almost non-existent in recent years. Retail sales in the market are only of coarse granulated white sugar No. 24, which costs 30 small silver dollars per load, while local white sugar costs only 16 or 17 silver dollars, a difference of almost double. Even if foreign sugar can be imported tax-free, the cost per load is more than 16 silver dollars, which is equal to native sugar. This is the market situation. Even if the government does not intervene, sugar merchants will not mix it, let alone confiscate it. This is proved from the perspective of understanding. The transportation of Qinzhou and Lianzhou native sugar to Shanghai is carried out by sailing ships from various sugar production areas to Beihai, where sugar taxes are collected by the Sugar Tax Bureau, and the goods are inspected by the Beihai Customs, and then exported to Shanghai by ship. The goods must be reported separately to the Beihai Customs and the Sugar Tax Bureau for inspection, and the transit tax must be paid, and the clearance documents must be given before they can be released. After inspection and loading, the attached sugar merchants cannot ask about the sugar. It is only when the goods are shipped directly to Shanghai that the consignee reports to the customs for import. The procedure is so strict that sugar merchants cannot mix foreign sugar with native sugar. This is proved from the perspective of fact. However, the Jianghai Customs still suspects that the Huainan native sugar shipped to Shanghai is transferred from Hong Kong and mixed. This is dare not to be said in other places where native sugar is expensive, or where it is transferred at will without inspection, and which takes Hong Kong as a gateway. However, under the above-mentioned special circumstances, the sugar merchants of Qinzhou and Lianzhou really cannot and will not borrow at all. In July last year, the native sugar attached by the sugar merchants Henghelong and other companies was fined four times, and it was all attached to Taikoo Steamship, which arrived in Shanghai from the original packaging in Beihai. It only temporarily anchored in Hong Kong and did not change ships for transfer. The native sugar carried by Yisun Wheel attached by Heli on August 28 went directly from Beihai to Shanghai and did not involve Hong Kong. Therefore, the suspicion of Jianghai Customs that it was transferred and mixed from Hong Kong is just a counter-evidence that the sugar merchants in Qinzhou and Lianzhou did not mix it at all. (Request Purpose) Based on the above facts and reasons, the petitioners have made a request in October last year, running around and appealing, and waiting for orders to suspend business. They originally hoped that those who were wronged by customs officials would be seen by the government. However, the Customs Administration has not yet conducted a detailed investigation, and only based on the report from the Inspector General of Customs and the Jianghai Customs, it has rejected the request, which is difficult to accept. He has always admired your Excellency for sympathizing with the difficulties of merchants, diligently seeking people's privacy, and for maintaining the industry in the past. He is using all his energy to state the details again and file an appeal in accordance with the law, respectfully asking you to conduct a thorough inspection and give special relief, revoke the decision of the Customs Administration, and accommodate the following requests: (1) Send personnel to the sugar production area of ​​Qinzhou and Lianzhou to conduct an on-site inspection, or allow the petitioner to collect sugar samples that have been publicly certified by local party and government agencies, mass groups, and send them to Beijing for inspection, and formulate measures to protect the safety of native sugar transit. (2) Order the Inspector General of Customs to return the fines and supplementary taxes in this case, and pray for their speedy implementation. Not only will the sugar merchants feel the injustice of Xue Fupen, but the future of customs administration will also be rectified. It is really for the convenience of both public morality. Respectfully submitted to the Minister of Finance Kong.

Xing Juefei Talks About the Petition Process of Hainan Sugar 128

The Guarantee Case Has Been Approved by the Executive Yuan

The Redress Case is Still Being Reviewed

Xin Sheng News Agency reported that the sugar merchants of Hainan Island had repeatedly been detained, fined, and confiscated by the Jianghai Customs of Hainan Island when they transported sugar to Shanghai, causing the merchants to suffer and be unable to appeal. They sent representative Yao Xing Juefei to Beijing to petition for redress and guarantee. It is now heard that the petition conditions have come to an end, and Representative Xing has returned to Shanghai. The reporter also learned the details and reported them to the readers. He specially visited Xing at the Yuegong Hotel on North Sichuan Road. According to Xing, the petition process is as follows: This time, I was entrusted by the sugar merchants of Hainan Island and the Chamber of Commerce of Haikou City to go to Beijing to state the suffering of sugar merchants and sugarcane farmers to the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Finance, the Customs Administration, and the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, and to appeal for guarantees. I was fortunate to have Premier Wang consider the people's livelihood, and accepted the advice of the lowly, and ordered the two ministries of Finance and Industry to handle this case together. Under the order of the two ministries, after several months of investigation, they have understood the crux of the problem, and after consultation, the following points have been made for the guarantee case: (1) Change the customs' sugar inspection standard, (2) Determine that the inspection power lies with the Hainan Customs. These two points really give merchants a lot of convenience. As for the redress case, the cases of Hesheng Jusheng will be handled separately, and it is proposed to mitigate the judgment to comfort the merchants' difficulties. For Yongcheng Qiongtai and Qiong Faxiang, the Ministry of Finance wants to maintain the original case, but I think that the Ministry of Finance cannot be fair in making amends, so I went to the Executive Yuan again to request that 40% of the supplementary tax be settled, and the confiscated and auctioned funds be returned to show fairness and convince the people. The President of the Executive Yuan also believes that this request is not without reason, so he ordered the Ministry of Finance to review it again for approval. This is the process of the petition case. However, this result depends entirely on the help of the national public opinion community, and the Shanghai Business Federation, the Shanghai City Chamber of Commerce, and the Guangdong Fellow Association in Shanghai have also sent telegrams to strongly urge the central government to protect domestic products and maintain the Hainan native sugar, which has attracted the attention of the authorities. This is what I am very grateful for. Now that the case has come to an end, I will return to Hainan to report everything in a few days, but because the journey is in a hurry, I have not been able to say goodbye one by one, which is really a pity.

Citywide Boy Scouts Present Commemorative Tower to Mayor Wu Yesterday

Ceremony Held at the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce Yesterday Afternoon

Wu Delivers Speech Encouraging Striving for Survival

The Shanghai Boy Scouts Council and the citywide Boy Scouts, recognizing Shanghai Mayor Wu Tiecheng's tireless efforts in promoting the Boy Scout movement, raised funds to purchase a bronze commemorative tower. The tower was presented to Mayor Wu at a ceremony held yesterday at 3 PM in the auditorium of the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce. Details of the event are as follows:

Attendees　The ceremony was attended by Mayor Wu Tiecheng, the recipient of the tower; Director Pan of the Bureau of Education; Tong Xingbai, Qu Yue, Wang Gang, and Leng Xueqiao of the Boy Scouts Council; and over 1,000 representatives from Boy Scout troops citywide. The presidium consisted of Tong Xingbai and Pan Gongzhan.

Qu Yue, Leng Xueqiao, Wang Gang, Conductor Sun Fuxin, Master of Ceremonies Luo Lie, Recorder Xie Yanbo, Disciplinary Officer Gong Jingyuan, Reception Zhao Weizu, Registration Zhou Mingshi and Wu Gang. Representatives presenting the tower were Yu Ming from Boy Scout Troop 349, Bao Ruixin from Girl Scout Troop 196, Gan Yuanda from Cub Scout Troop 177, Xing Li from Rover Scout Crew 270, and Shen Yu representing the staff.

Citywide Boy Scouts Present Commemorative Tower　(Photo by Qi Chang)

Venue Arrangement　The venue was the auditorium of the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce on Tianhougong Bridge. A white cloth banner reading "Citywide Boy Scouts Present Commemorative Tower" was hung in front of the stage. The commemorative tower stood below the stage, surrounded by colorful paper streamers. The atmosphere was orderly and solemn. Boy Scouts stood guard along the route at the entrance. The Shanghai Municipal Police sent a military band to play music at the venue.

Construction of the Bronze Tower　The tower was designed by Wang Gang of the Boy Scouts Council and cast by the Juvenile Supplies Supply Company at a cost of 200 yuan. It is made of bronze with a purple hue, stands three feet tall, and has a base diameter of one foot. It features a censer foot and a gourd-shaped top, with two sets of steps leading up in succession, totaling seven levels. Each level has six sides, resembling a palace with complete doors, windows, and distinct roof tiles. The entire structure is exquisitely crafted. When struck, it produces a resounding sound. On the lower section of the front of the tower, there are three lines of white characters: the top line reads "Presented to Mr. Wu Tiecheng, Mayor of Shanghai," the middle line reads "The Shanghai Special Municipality Council of the Boy Scouts of China," and the bottom line reads "Presented by the Heads of Various Troops and the Citywide Boy Scouts." On the back, three lines are engraved with the mottoes "Be Prepared," "Do a Good Turn Daily," and "Service to Humanity is the Purpose of Life." The left and right sides are engraved with the twelve Boy Scout Laws: Honesty, Loyalty, Helpfulness, Kindness, Courtesy, Fairness, Obedience, Cheerfulness, Thrift, Bravery, Cleanliness, and Public Spirit, which are quite

deeply engraved.

Presentation Speech　The Boy Scouts Council prepared a special presentation speech to express their sincerity.

The text reads, "We, the Shanghai Boy Scouts, have observed that since your arrival in office, Mr. Mayor, you have spared no effort in promoting and supporting our cause. Your perseverance and enthusiasm are deeply appreciated. Therefore, we have pooled the modest resources of the citywide Boy Scouts to cast this ancient tower as a respectful gift to commemorate your contributions and express our admiration. Respectfully presented to Mr. Wu Tiecheng, Mayor of Shanghai, by the Shanghai Council of the Boy Scouts of China, representing the citywide Boy Scouts, March 10, 1934."

Ceremony Held　When Mayor Wu Tiecheng arrived, Conductor Sun Yixin signaled with a bugle, and all the attending Boy Scouts stood at attention and saluted. Then, the meeting was opened with the ringing of a bell. After the formalities, the Chairman first reported the purpose of the meeting, followed by the presentation of the tower to Mayor Wu by representatives of the Girl Scouts, Bao Ruixin, the leader of the 196th troop, the Rover Scouts, the leader of the 270th troop, the Cub Scouts, Gan Yuanda, the leader of the 177th troop, the Boy Scouts, Yu Peng, the leader of the 349th troop, and Shen Yu, a staff member. After Mayor Wu received the tower, he delivered a speech of thanks, followed by speeches by Pan Gongzhan and others. The ceremony concluded with a group photograph and adjournment.

Chairman's Report　Chairman Tong Xingbai reported, in brief, that,

Today, the Shanghai Citywide Boy Scouts

hold a presentation ceremony of the tower. This fact breaks the record of all past activities. Since Mayor Wu took office, his advocacy for the Boy Scout cause has been unprecedented, enabling significant progress in the city's Boy Scout movement and providing encouragement to the citywide Boy Scouts. Therefore, the citywide Boy Scouts voluntarily donated funds to purchase this commemorative tower to express our gratitude.

The old saying goes, "Many grains of sand make a tower". This action deeply matches its meaning. Mayor Wu once said to me that he intended to carry out outdoor activities with the citywide Boy Scouts, which showed Mayor Wu's concern for the Boy Scout cause, and to live together. This is something that we are grateful for. If we want to restore the glory of the country, we must first seek the revival of the nation. To revive the nation, we must first eliminate the bad habits of the nation. The New Life Movement advocated by Chairman Chiang is based on this. All the rules of the Boy Scouts are also to wash away China's old bad habits and create a new life. I believe that the Boy Scout life should not only be universal in the entire student community, but also be popularized to the entire nation. With Mayor Wu's love for the Boy Scouts, we should encourage each other to create a bright future for the Boy Scout movement.

Mayor's Speech　In brief, he said, "Today, the Shanghai Boy Scout community holds this grand ceremony. I consider this the most honorable thing in my life, but at the same time, I cannot help but feel fearful. What is honorable is that the Chairman said that this is a pioneering event in the Boy Scout community in the past ten years. This action did not come from the Council or the leaders of various troops, but was purely initiated by the citywide Boy Scouts. Therefore, I deeply feel that this is the most honorable thing in my life. What is fearful is that although I am a revolutionary, I should take the revival of the Chinese nation as my own responsibility, and I should work hard to complete this mission. The starting point and foundation of national revival is the Boy Scout movement. The revolutionary party has an unshirkable duty to the Boy Scout movement. Although it is necessary to work hard, due to time and government affairs, I have not been able to devote all my efforts to this. Now, I am receiving such a grand commemorative gift. How can I not feel ashamed? Therefore, in the past, I really felt ashamed, and in the future, I will feel even more fearful. Therefore, I will make this memorial object my motto, so that I can be reminded and stimulated at any time to work hard for the mission of the revolution. For this starting point and basic work of national revival, such as the Boy Scout movement, I should be more self-motivated and work hard. I still have a few words to offer to you, and I hope that you can pass these words on to your relatives and friends. Today, the people of the whole country all take survival as the most urgent task. The so-called survival is the New Life Movement advocated by Chairman Chiang in Nanchang. The so-called survival is nothing more than turning China into a new era of country, so that it has the strength to survive and can compete with other countries for survival. Make the bronze tower a miniature of the new era　(Photo by Gong Shuxian)

A country should pay attention to the modernization of the life of the entire nation. Today, the Chinese people have two extremely contradictory lifestyles: one is easily seen in cities, where life is extremely extravagant and hedonistic; the other is easily seen in the inland, where life is extremely miserable. Both of these violate the original meaning of the new era of life. The so-called new era of life should have a spirit of hard work, endurance, perseverance, and decisiveness. On the one hand, it aims to reduce the suffering of people's lives, and on the other hand, it cannot make them fall into extravagance and follow the footsteps of people in developed industrial countries in Europe and the United States. Since we take the revival of the nation as our mission, we should work hard to complete this mission, and we should pay more attention to the starting point and basic work of this national revival, such as the Boy Scout movement. In addition to expressing my gratitude, I will also use this memorial object as my motto to stimulate and remind me not to forget the important work in the process of national revival."

Joining the Boy Scouts　When the ceremony was about to end, Mayor Wu officially announced to the public that he was joining the Boy Scouts. Tong Xingbai and Pan Gongzhan also joined at the same time. The Boy Scout representatives applauded and cheered in unison.

Duan Qirui to Leave Shanghai to Avoid Birthday Celebrations 133

March 23rd, which is the ninth day of the second month of the lunar calendar, is Duan Qirui's 70th birthday. Many of his former students and officials from various provinces wanted to come to Shanghai to offer him wine and celebrate his birthday. However, Duan believes that the country is facing many difficulties and the people are suffering. This is not a time for personal birthday celebrations. He has decided to decline all celebrations and recalls that in the past few decades, he has always strictly refused celebrations on his birthdays. This is well known at home and abroad. Therefore, he has recently strictly instructed his family not to hold any celebrations, perform operas, or accept any gifts on that day. It is also heard that he plans to go to a certain monastery that day to fast and worship Buddha.

Shanghai Municipal Council Considers Tax Exemption Requests 142

The Shanghai Chinese YMCA at 599 Sichuan Road raised an objection because the estimated donation amount had increased. After consideration by the Municipal Council, it was decided that the request could not be approved. Since the YMCA already receives a subsidy from the Municipal Council for education, it was decided to treat it the same as the Western YMCA, collecting the full amount of the donation but allowing a 10% reduction.

For the house at 1274 Jing'an Temple Road, the assessed rental value was 4,800 yuan, and the resident raised an objection. After consideration by the Finance Committee, it was decided that the assessed value of the house had been very low for many years and the discount had been in place for a long time. The newly determined assessed value could not be changed again.

Guangren Hospital rented the house at No. 21, Lane 608, Chengdu Road for hospital use and requested exemption from the general donation. The Municipal Council decided to approve it.

The Jiangnan Missionary Society (translated name) requested that two pieces of land occupied by them be exempted from land tax. After deliberation by the Finance Committee, it was decided that this tax exemption could only be limited to the land occupied by the church. Other buildings were not covered by this rule. Therefore, it was decided that out of the total land tax of 4609.69 yuan payable by the society, 89.1.34 yuan would be exempted. The above cases have all been approved by the board of directors and will be implemented accordingly.

Emergency Meeting of the 17th Branch of the Municipal Federation 143

Wu Yong'an's Fraud Discovered

Write to the Court for Severe Punishment

The Xin Sheng News Agency reports that the 17th District Branch of the Shanghai Special First District Citizens' Union held its fifth executive committee meeting at its office on Sichuan Road at 2 PM yesterday. Guo Ruowen, Lin Shaoqiao, Lian Rongjiang,

Yan Jingwen, Wang Jian'e, Chen Minglai, Chen Jiufeng (Jiang representing), Yu Mingxun, Zhao Zhiyan, Li Qianheng, Tang Huilian, and others attended, totaling eleven people. Yu Mingxun was elected as chairman. After performing the formalities, the chairman reported that Wu Yong'an had defrauded money in the name of the association, which was related to the reputation of the association. Therefore, an emergency meeting was called to discuss the handling method.

Fraud Details Next, Wang Jian'e reported that on the evening of the 7th, a man named Wu Yong'an, accompanied by detectives from the Shanghai Municipal Police, came to the apartment to inquire because Wu Yong'an had fraudulently convened a so-called rent reduction movement for the Xinshunli, Yixingli, Yuqingli, Shenyuli, and Xujia Garden, all in the name of the 17th District Branch of the Citizens' Union. On the one hand, he charged a membership fee of one yuan to each shop and resident, and according to his confession, he had asked Jian'e for instructions. At that time, Jian'e was not at the apartment, and later learned about it, and was deeply shocked. Wu Yong'an was in the same company as Jian'e and was under his jurisdiction, but Jian'e regarded him as just one of the staff members. In the past, during conversations, he had asked Jian'e about the rent reduction movement and the organization of district branches, and was told that rent reduction must be initiated by the tenants themselves and must comply with the law and order. For example, the rent reduction proposal of the 17th District Citizens' Association is to gather the opinions of the majority of tenants and first negotiate with the landlord within the possible range. If you want to organize a district branch, you must submit it to the General Association, and then ask the party and government organs to approve the record, which is legal. Whoever intended Wu Yong'an to be harboring evil intentions, privately carved seals, printed receipts, and collected membership fees. This is not only unknown to Jian'e, but also conflicts with the resolution of the second executive supervisory committee meeting on January 22 that no fees will be charged externally. Now that Wu Yong'an has been arrested for committing a crime and has also shifted the blame on others, he is extremely illegal. From the standpoint of the district branch, we should study the methods of dealing with it and give it severe sanctions.

Resolution Methods Next, the discussion began to record the motion. (1) Wu Yong'an from Anhui fraudulently obtained money in the name of the association from Xinshunli, etc. on Tiantong Road outside the scope of the district. The court has already prosecuted, and how should the association claim it? The resolution, Wu Yong'an's fraudulent money in the name of the outside has been prosecuted by the court, and the association should send a letter to the court in the name of the executive committee to severely sanction it. (2) All external actions of the association are signed and sealed by the daily standing committee. Should we notify all members again to avoid misunderstandings? Resolved, notify again. (3) The association's organization of the rent reduction movement was resolved at the second executive supervisory committee meeting on January 23, and no fees will be charged externally. Should we make another statement? Resolved, the association's organization of the rent reduction movement is at the request of the citizens, in order to adapt to the social environment, so it is to relieve the pain as the first righteousness, and never

increase the burden on citizens, so all expenses are borne by the association. Now, in order to clarify the truth to all sectors, we will solemnly declare again, so that we can inform everyone.

He studied diligently, determined to delve into research, his scholarship and conduct were outstanding, surpassing his peers. He strived for further studies, went to America, worked hard, and spent many years. He followed Christ, respected Heaven and loved others, compassionate and kind, bringing spring to all things. Our Lord said, "Blessed are those who give, not to be served, but to serve." You followed this teaching, established the Hudong Commune, resolved disputes and difficulties, and benefited laborers. You spoke in the halls, your voice was loud and clear, your words flowed like a river, and everyone felt like spring. For ten years of hard work, you were as one day. No one doubted your loyalty and integrity. With a robust physique and in the prime of life, you suddenly returned to Heaven due to a tooth ailment. Alas, Mr. Qian, you were a rare talent in this era, knowledgeable and insightful, yet you did not live long. Your old mother is in the hall, your wife is in the chamber, one son and seven daughters, alas, where do they turn? The cold wind is chilling, the setting sun is pale, a wise man has withered, our hearts are filled with sorrow. We have been through thick and thin together, not just for a day or a night. We dare to present these rough words to bid farewell to your tomb.' Finally, the students of the Hudong Commune sang a mournful song, the tone was sad and moving, making people feel heartbroken. After Qian's family expressed their gratitude, the meeting adjourned until after five o'clock."

Public Concession Bureau Candidate Director 布莽 Unexpectedly Has Bad Deeds Published by Russian Newspaper 148

Great Impact on 布莽's Election This Year

Lawyer Jiang Yiping Sues the Newspaper's Editor

布莽 (transliteration), a Belgian citizen residing at No. 15 Museum Road in the Public Concession, an American citizen, is the editor-in-chief of an English magazine. He has a good reputation in Shanghai society and is one of the candidate directors of the Western taxpayers' meeting of the Public Concession Bureau. The election will be held in March of this year, and he has hope of being elected. Unexpectedly, on February 7th and 8th, the Russian-language newspaper "考克筆" (transliteration, meaning "a penny" in Russian), located on Avenue Joffre in the French Concession, published

unflattering stories about 布莽's life, including defamatory language. 布莽 was shocked upon reading the newspaper. Because the newspaper publicly spread defamatory words, it had a great impact on his election and harmed his lifelong reputation. Therefore, he hired lawyer Jiang Yiping to represent him and filed a complaint with the Criminal Court of the Second Special District Court, accusing the Russian editor of "考克筆" newspaper, 吉列根 (transliteration), of defamation and requesting a legal investigation. The court accepted the complaint and summoned both parties at 11:30 am yesterday. Judge Wu Fanglian presided over the hearing in the Second Criminal Court. First, lawyer Jiang Yiping, the agent of the plaintiff, stated the intention of the lawsuit and presented the newspaper as evidence. The defendant, 吉列根, was defended by lawyer Zhang Jiawei, who stated that the words in the defendant's newspaper were completely based on facts and contained no defamation. He requested the court to investigate with Mr. Zhong Si, the general manager of the British Public Concession Bureau, which would clarify everything. He also listed several witnesses and requested that they be summoned. The judge believed that the newspaper still needed to be translated and that it was necessary to investigate the case, so he ordered the hearing to be adjourned until a later date.

United Benefit Association of Fishery Merchants Protects Fish Fry Merchants 149

Yesterday's Meeting of Directors and Supervisors

Petitioning the Government to Reiterate Prohibition Orders

Last year, the Shanghai Fishery Merchants United Benefit Association accepted the request of fish fry merchants for protection and immediately prepared a document to the Ministry of Industry, requesting that an order be issued for protection. The Ministry of Industry then sent a letter to the Ministry of Military Affairs and the Ministry of Interior, respectively ordering the governments of Jiangxi, Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, and Hubei provinces to instruct their subordinate military and police agencies to provide strict protection. Therefore, fish fry merchants traveling along the Yangtze River were not extorted by hooligans or others. In Shanghai, the association also submitted a petition to the party and government agencies in advance, requesting that the Public Security Bureau's water patrol team be instructed to send police to escort them when the time came. Therefore, last year, the fish fry merchants deeply appreciated the government agencies' effective protection. The fish fry season is approaching again this year. Recently, fish fry gang leaders such as Ji Debao sent a telegram to the association, requesting that petitions be sent to the government again to reiterate the prohibition orders, so as to avoid the loss of effectiveness over time and the merchants suffering losses. The association specially convened a meeting of directors and supervisors yesterday, attended by Zhu Yangwu, Zhou Lianze, Shen Mingzhe, He Zongnian, Chen Ganfu, Yao Xingdao, (He Dai) Chu Genfu, Lu Weixin, Zhang Lansheng, Zhang Yuxiu, Wu Longsheng, and others. Discussions: (1) Shi Changfa and others requested to join the association because they could not withstand the extortion by hooligans in the Songjiang waters. It was resolved to send someone to investigate the truth and then review the matter. (2) The fish fry season is approaching, and how should protection be provided? It was resolved: (1) To petition the Ministry of Industry; (2) To petition the Municipal Government, the Municipal Party Department, and the Social Affairs Bureau; (3) To petition the Municipal Government to consult with the French Consul, instructing the French Concession police to provide protection. The section on loans is omitted.

Three Robberies in One Day 150

Datong Road: Yesterday at around 5 pm, five robbers suddenly came to a certain family at No. 276 Datong Road. Two of the robbers had handguns, and three robbers guarded the front and back doors. The two armed robbers entered the house, told everyone to be quiet, and ordered the owner to hand over the keys to the boxes. They then went to each room, overturned boxes and chests, and looted at will. After about half an hour, they left with their loot. However, at this time, the owner saw that the shape of the handguns held by the two robbers was different. Upon closer inspection, they were fake. Just as he was about to find a way to capture them, the robbers had already fled. The owner hurriedly chased out, but saw that there were still accomplices outside the door. Fearing an ambush, he did not dare to make a sound. He returned to check the losses, which amounted to more than 1,700 yuan. He quickly reported to the police station in charge, requesting an arrest.

Aidoa Road: Yesterday at 7:20 pm, six robbers suddenly went to a certain business at No. 98 Aidoa Road. Four of them had handguns, and two were unarmed. After entering the shop, they shouted at the shop assistants and forbade them from making a sound. Two robbers walked into the counter to rob, and two other robbers broke into the upstairs, rummaging through each room. After about twenty minutes, they each fled with their loot. After checking, it was estimated that they had been robbed of banknotes, jewelry, clothes, etc., in a considerable amount. The owner reported to the police station, which sent detectives to investigate and search everywhere.

Daxi Road: At 9 am this morning, three robbers suddenly went to a certain family at No. 23 Rongkang Lane on Daxi Road. Two robbers guarded the front and back doors, and the armed robber entered the house, threatening the owner to hand over the keys to the boxes and let them search at will. The Grand Lantern Festival Held in Caohejing for Three Days 151

Three Kinds of Ceremonies Held Simultaneously

Lanterns Were Splendid and Unprecedented

Caohejing Town in West Shanghai suffered repeated military disasters in the past, and all places were ravaged. Only Caohejing was protected by the leader of the defense group, Yang Xinzheng, who took on the arduous task of entertaining soldiers and maintaining order. The whole town relied on him to be safe and sound. Local people praised him. Therefore, every year on March 8, 9, and 13 (that is, the 23rd, 24th, and 25th days of the Lunar New Year), lanterns are hung for three days to celebrate. This year is the tenth anniversary, and it also coincides with the opening of the Caojin Road, the completion of the Jinrong Bridge, and the establishment of the Huangjia Garden Fire Brigade. Various ceremonies are held simultaneously. A total of seven archways are decorated with lanterns in the east, west, north, and south. Every archway has couplets written by celebrities. The couplet of the east archway says, "Auspicious clouds come from the east to see the bridge, the Golden Bridge welcomes the tide to Puwei. Huang Garden looks west with joy, the road connects to Caojin. The fire brigade is formed." The couplet of the west archway says, "Candlelight reflects the clear waves, several curves of the clear stream are initially dredged. Lantern light deceives the bright moon, a new road shines for speeding." The couplet of the central archway says, "Preventing disasters and defending against troubles, we celebrate the peace of one side. Everyone watches the people lighting lanterns." Another couplet says, "From east to west, everything we see is lanterns and streamers. From the center to the outside, we can travel and enjoy the singing."

The rest are too numerous to mention. At 7 pm, people from all walks of life participated in the lantern parade, including military bands, Jinrong School Boy Scouts, Huangjia Garden Fire Brigade, and various lanterns. The parade extended for more than three miles, and the audience was crowded. Along the way, there were security offices, public security bureaus, and military and police of the defense group, working together to maintain order.

Chinese Red Cross Society Hastens to Distribute Relief Rice in Zhabei 152

Due to the continuous fires in Zhabei, the Chinese Red Cross Society, led by Wen Lanting, Wang Buyuan, and others, convened a meeting and decided to hasten the distribution of emergency relief, as reported in various newspapers. Considering the large number of refugees, it was inevitable that there would be rice grabbing. In order to standardize the procedures, tens of thousands of rice tickets were specially made, each for four liters, and distributed according to the number of family members. People could collect rice with the tickets to avoid crowding. The names and addresses were registered when the tickets were collected for accounting purposes. The distribution began in the disaster area on the morning of the 10th.

Kidnapper Liu Ziyu Sentenced to Death in the Fan Aisheng Case 155

Qiu Yulou Sentenced to Thirteen Years

Fan Aisheng, manager of Dehe Public Indigo Company on Ningbo Road, lived at No. 31 Crow Road in the French Concession. On January 23 of this year, at 7:45 pm, while riding in his private chartered car, he was suddenly kidnapped by several kidnappers at the intersection of Guangxi Road and Shantou Road. The kidnappers demanded a huge ransom. Later, Yu A'gen, chief detective of the Old Gate Police Station, detectives Zhou Guisen and Zhang Yuanqing, and detective Shen Jinwen, arrested three kidnappers: Liu Ziyu from Shandong, Qiu Yulou from Jiangbei, and Cui Yaowen (also known as Ziming and Jinming) from Chongming. Fan was rescued at No. 10 Shunan Lane, West Aishi Road in the French Concession. When the detectives arrested Liu, Liu opened fire and resisted arrest. Detective Liu Ziliang was shot and injured. The case was sent to the First Special Court for interrogation and detention. Later, Cui Yaowen was released on bail due to illness. Yesterday morning, Chief Judge Qian Hongye of the Criminal Court opened a hearing. Cui Yaowen was unable to appear due to his inability to move. After a brief interrogation, the court ordered that the debate on the Liu and Qiu cases begin. After the Public Security Bureau's lawyer Li Zhishan and the defendants' defense counsel debated, Judge Qian announced the verdict in court. Liu Ziyu was sentenced to death for kidnapping and demanding ransom. Qiu Yulou was sentenced to thirteen years in prison for aiding and abetting kidnapping and demanding ransom. The number of days of detention before the final verdict was determined to be two days equal to one day of imprisonment. One handgun, glasses, seals, handcuffs, etc., were confiscated according to the list. The Cui Yaowen case was postponed for two weeks.

Shareholders' Meeting of the China National Products Company 159

The China National Products Company, located in the Continental Emporium on Nanjing Road, held its shareholders' meeting on the 10th of this month at the Lake Society on Beijing Road. Chairman Fang Yexian first reported on the company's business situation last year and the process of increasing capital. He briefly stated that since the company opened on February 9th last year, it felt that the original northern emporium was too small to meet the needs of customers. Therefore, it was decided at a special shareholders' meeting last year to establish a southern emporium. At the same time, due to the establishment of the southern emporium, it was decided to increase capital by 100,000 yuan. This capital was fully collected last year, and the southern emporium has already been established, etc. Next, he described the situation of purchasing goods, briefly stating that when the company was established, very few factories participated. After the southern emporium was established, the number of factories trading with the company reached 500, and to date it has exceeded 1,400. Among them, small factories account for the majority. Although their products are excellent, the market's recognition is still limited. Today, the company's promotion of their products is tantamount to opening up a new path for them, etc. Next, he described the sales situation, briefly stating that the company's sales methods include wholesale, mail order, and retail departments, with the retail department being the core of the business. The pricing of various goods strives to be low, so the results are still satisfactory. Now, national products emporiums and national products stores that have followed the company are everywhere, which may also be good news for the future of national products, etc. Next, he described the publicity work, such as holding the Chicago Exposition, the Children's Amusement Market, and the Fashion Show, etc., all of which had a good impression. Next, he described the financial and business situation, stating that with the enthusiastic support of all parties, everything was well-arranged and reassuring to the shareholders, etc. However, under the sluggish market conditions last year, the company was fortunate to have a slight surplus. In the future, as the market gradually turns around, colleagues should encourage themselves more and live up to the shareholders' trust, etc. Next, the supervisor Yan Fang reported on the account briefly. Next, there was the distribution of surplus, amendment of articles of association, and election of directors and supervisors. In addition to the re-elected directors Wang Zhixin, Ren Shigang, Cai Shengbai, Zhang Huikang, and Fang Yexian, six new directors were elected, namely Shi Liangcai, Shi Haifeng, Yan Fang, Pan Yangyao, Fang Jiange, and Ye Youcai. Bandit Li Chunsheng and Others Repeatedly Committed Murder Cases, All with Labor Union Political Connections 160

The families of the victims have had difficulties for many years in investigations.

Yesterday, the Yangshupu robbery case and the assassination case were heard first.

Wu Wanzhang appeared in court to testify about the shooting.

Detective Wang Cheng of the Chinese Detective Force and detective Yang Xiguang arrested four bandits, Cao Zhenxi, Xu Debiao, Du Baoliang, and Li Chunsheng, at the Dexinglou Restaurant at 1719 Tangen Road at 12:30 am on the 24th of last month. A pistol and eight bullets were found on Cao. Subsequently, two accomplices, Tang Xuyou and Ma Linxiang, were captured and brought to the police station. They confessed to robbing a residence at No. 5 Donglai Lane, Yangshupu Road, in September last year, stealing dozens of silver dollars worth of property. It was also investigated that these people, at approximately 4:00 am on January 22nd of this year, led a gang to rob the Derenhua Products Factory at No. 914 Gonghe New Road, Zhabei, and opened fire, killing the manager, Tang Xiangshou, a Ningbo native. Subsequently, it was found that Li Chunsheng, on December 12th of the 18th year of the Republic of China, colluded with Xia Shaoqiu, Gu Rufang, Ding Yunsheng, Liu Shanzhou, and Wang Ruiting, Fu Shatang, to assassinate Xie Baosheng (also known as A Bao), an Anhui native, on Putuo Road. Xie was a foreman at an internal and external cotton yarn factory. The defendants were separately escorted by the Jiaxing Road Police Station to the First Special District Court for interrogation and detention. It was found that Li Chunsheng, Fu Shatang, and others had joined the labor union, advocating for the overthrow of capitalism. In addition to murdering Xie A Bao, they had also colluded with the already arrested and punished leader Kong Guangfu between December of the 15th year of the Republic of China and March of the 17th year of the Republic of China, successively killing Dai Dianchen, Shi Jinkun, Zhang Liangcai, a woman named Bao Dongshi, and Wu Wanzhang, a Hubei native, on Putuo Road, Gordon Road, and Tokyo Road. Wu Wanzhang was also shot and wounded, but fortunately did not die. There were a total of six incidents, all related to political connections. Yesterday morning, the police sent Cao Zhenxi, Fu Shaotang, and others to the Third Criminal Court. Wang Yaotang, a lawyer from the Public Works Department, stated that in addition to the Xie Baosheng murder case, the other five cases had not yet been prosecuted due to incomplete procedures. It takes considerable time to investigate and summon the families of the victims. Only Wu Wanzhang has appeared in court. Now, after questioning Cao Zhenxi about the Yangshupu robbery case and Wu's attempted murder case, the hearing will be postponed for further investigation, and a special hearing will be scheduled, etc. The court approved it. According to the defendant Tang Xuyou, the Yangshupu robbery case in September last year was committed by two fugitives named Zhang and Liu. He did not receive any money. At approximately 3:00 pm on February 23rd of this year, the pistol carried by Cao was not his property. Xu Debiao stated that according to Zhang, the pistol in the Yangshupu robbery case belonged to Tang Xu. Cao Zhenxi stated that the firearm seized from him was given to him by Li Chunsheng to take to Hongkou, promising to pay him three yuan. Li Chunsheng stated that he had a feud with a man named Yang Wenzhun and instructed Cao to falsely accuse him. Subsequently, his mother, Li Lu, testified that Yang Wenzhun had a feud with her son and promised Cao a reward of fifty yuan to implicate him. Cao denied this. Next, the investigation of the attempted assassination of Wu Wanzhang case proceeded. According to Wu, he worked as an inspector in an internal and external yarn factory, but did not join the labor union. He lived near Deyou Lane, Putuo Road, and had a lecture hall. Fu Shaotang also worked as an inspector. Prior to the incident, Fu came to Wu's house, and on the third occasion, invited Wu to give a speech at the lecture hall. Wu went with his wife and family. As soon as they entered the lane of the lecture hall, they suddenly heard a gunshot from behind, and a bullet struck Wu's neck, exiting from the front. The second shot hit Wu's wife's arm. Turning around, he saw a short person wearing a blue cloth shirt and pants, and a peaked cap, fleeing north. Fu then sent Wu to the hospital for treatment. Later, he entrusted Gu Rufang, also a colleague, to inquire with the labor union about the attempted murder. It was said that the shooter was named Wang A San, and the reason was that Wu was considered a running dog of the capitalists and had not joined the labor union, so he was shot. If he paid 100 silver dollars and hosted a banquet, there would be no further trouble. According to Gu Rufang, Wang Ruiting informed him of this matter, and it was instigated by a Kong. Wu was to be beaten to death. The shooter was said to be Tao San, etc. Li Chunsheng denied shooting and committing the crime. Wu Wanzhang stated that he admitted at the police station that a Shen from the labor union had ordered him to be shot. Moreover, the person who shot him at that time was of the same stature as Li Chunsheng. Fu Shaotang initially denied being an accomplice, but later stated that the matter was under the orders of Kong Guangfu, a key figure in the labor union, and Zhang Jianyou was instructed to lure Wu to the lecture hall lane to carry out the act. He was truly unable to disobey the labor union's orders and had no choice, pleading for consideration. Judge Xiao Xiezhen ordered the defendants to be remanded in custody and rescheduled the hearing for the afternoon of the 23rd of this month for further verification.

Traveler Commits Suicide in Pingqiao Hotel 169

Ding Linsheng, a native of Changshu, 25 years old, made a living as a carpenter. At about 11 o'clock the night before last, he checked into room 46 of the Pingqiao Hotel on Pingqiao Road. Traveler Rescued After Taking Poison 173

At around 7:00 pm on the 7th, a traveler resembling a businessman came to the Pacific Hotel at No. 430 Guangxi Road to check in. The hotel's accountant led him to room 22. He claimed his name was Yang Rengen, 28 years old, a local, and he had no luggage or other items. For several days, he went to bed early and got up early, stayed indoors, and there were no abnormalities. However, yesterday he did not get up until noon. He immediately called the waiter into the room and asked him to bring some cold water. The waiter asked if he wanted lunch, but he shook his head and said, "I still need to take a nap." He told him to call him again at 7:00 pm. The waiter agreed and left, and Yang closed the door and went to sleep. At 7:00 pm in the evening, the waiter went to knock on the door on time, but there was no response for a long time. He then opened the door and went inside, and saw Yang lying across the bed, his face pale. On the table in the room, there was an empty box of red phosphorus matches. Asking him what happened, he was evasive. The waiter hurriedly reported to the accounting room, who reported to the police station. The detective sent Yang to Renji Hospital for treatment. After the hospital doctor rescued him, he found that he had taken a tranquilizer and then swallowed red phosphorus to commit suicide. Fortunately, he vomited it out shortly after, and his life was not in danger. After he woke up, he claimed that his real name was Yang Rengen and he was from Hangzhou. When asked why he wanted to commit suicide, he firmly refused to tell the truth.

Reading Q&A

On the Steps of Literary Study, Writing, and Others (2) 179

Above, we have done a check on the plans of Wang, Chen, Guo, and Jin to study literature, and briefly shown our criticism of them. Below, we put forward some more specific opinions to consult with the general readers. Editor

In principle, our plan for studying literature, no matter what steps we take, should be preliminary, introductory, general, and conceptual in the overall aspect. We cannot set the scope too wide or too high now, so as not to be out of touch with reality in application. We are not saying that there should absolutely not be too broad and too high a scope; however, that is a further step. After the "preliminary, introductory, general, and conceptual" has a "considerable foundation," you can find your way around in your research. At that time, no matter how high and broad your plans are, you can also have methods to deal with them properly. We learn from each other's strengths and make up for each other's weaknesses, and contribute a preliminary research plan for you with our own opinions.

First Phase | Focus on reading a few introductions to literature, dozens of works of creation, and exploring the basic knowledge of social sciences.

Second Phase | Focus on the study of literary theory.

Third Phase | In addition to continuing to deepen the above two research items, also explore creative methods.

Books to read in the first phase, for the basic knowledge part of social science, you can refer to the book list listed in the "Preliminary Reading of Social Sciences" article in this column on February 21, 22, and 23.

There are many literary theory books to read in the second phase. Let's list a few:

㈠ Theory of Art, Dajiang Edition

㈡ Modern Literary Trends, Kaiming Edition

㈢ Collection of Essays on New Realism, Modern Edition

㈣ Sociological Research on Literature, Dajiang Edition

㈤ Various Problems of Modern Emerging Literature, Dajiang Edition

㈥ Criticism of Literary Studies, Shuimo Edition

Books to read in the third phase on literary creation methods:

㈠ On Composition, Commercial Press Edition

㈡ Creative Experience, Tianma Edition

㈢ Literary and Artistic Technical Revolution, Dajiang Edition

As for the selection of literary works to be read in each period, in our opinion: read modern first and then ancient, and take into account both domestic creations and translations from foreign countries. This meaning has been explained before, so I will not repeat it. Modern Chinese writers such as Zhou Zuoren, Zhou Shuren, Guo Moruo, Tian Han, Hong Shen, Ding Ling, Ba Jin, Shen Congwen: : : and others' creations; translated works such as Ibsen and Shaw's dramas, Sinclair, Gorky, Remarque, Serafimovich, Fadeev and others' novels.

Of course, there are more than just these few people's things that can be read: but based on the readers' time, learning ability, etc., it is impossible to come up with a book list that everyone thinks is completely flawless. Readers should remember that Liang Rengong and Hu Shi fought a big ink battle a few years ago because of drafting a national studies book list, but it ended without results. But a multi-faceted book list is still useful, even though it is very miscellaneous or very incomplete. When you go to a restaurant for dinner, the restaurant gives you a menu. Although you still have to listen to the diners' own choices and decisions, people who don't often go to restaurants can't order dishes.

Next, let's talk about writing. Chen Jun's questions are: ㈠ Before starting to write, is it right to first stipulate the meaning of the writing, that is, the central idea? ㈡ After writing well, I often feel that I still cannot express four-tenths of what I want to write, so I destroy it all. Should this kind of behavior be done?

For the first question, we will talk about it in two levels. First, the work should have its central idea, which is the law of nature. The so-called central idea is the content. Without content, it is not a work, but just the literary game of boring literati that we mentioned above. Second, the production process of general works is that social reality is reflected in the writer's nerve center and gradually condenses into an idea. Then, it is copied to paper in concrete images: as shown in the following table: Reality ↓ Idea ↓ Work Writer's idea concrete expression ←→ Reality. It is reality that stipulates your central idea, not you yourself who can create a central idea out of thin air. The central idea has not yet condensed in your brain. In other words, you don't even know what to write well before you write it, and the result is that you have experienced a miscarriage.

For the second question, we assume that Chen Jun has a central idea before he starts writing, then Chen Jun's spirit of seeking perfection is admirable. This kind of manuscript destruction is not only a common phenomenon for beginners, but also for writers who have been famous all over the world from ancient times to the present. (Please refer to the Reading and Q&A on March 4, 5, 6, and 7: Reading and Writing) We don't think this is a failure and become discouraged: With the effort to seek perfection: one day you can climb the road to success, but we still have a word to say to Chen Jun: It is best not to destroy the unsatisfactory manuscript, and keep it to review it when you have time. Modify it slowly little by little, and sometimes these things will become useful with the increase of your experience and skills. For example, when sewing new clothes, having old clothes as a base for reference, it is easier to measure the new clothes to fit.

Jin Jun said: "The more difficult my position is and the more difficult it is to study, the more determined my will to seek knowledge! For myself, for the way out of the whole society. I struggle, and I try my best to struggle: : :" This makes us really happy. However, in this regard, Jin Jun is still like the letters from many readers. He loves literature. However, on the one hand, he feels that it is "presumptuous" for a busy person like him to love literature. On the other hand, he dislikes the hard life of literature and wants to give it up, but he can't give it up. This is a contradiction. If Jin Jun and other friends who love literature don't regard literature as something that high-ranking hermits in the "ivory tower" use to chant poems and play with the moon, then how can there be so-called presumption or non-presumption? If culture is not related to our busy people, this kind of culture is undesirable. Since we regard our pursuit of knowledge as struggling for ourselves and for the way out of the whole society, then what is there to dislike about being poor?

We still hope that you will continue to study with your original intention.

Many readers complained in their letters after raising certain questions that they had repeatedly submitted articles to publications but had not received the glory of publication. Many people have therefore been discouraged from practicing writing. Gao Ping said: "People who are a little familiar with the current situation of the Chinese publishing industry should know that 99% of the manuscripts of unknown writers will not be favored by editors. The reason is not in the "quality" of the works of unknown writers. No, few of our editor gentlemen are willing to take a look at the works of unknown writers. A well-intentioned explanation is that the general editors are too busy and don't have time to do the work of "sifting sand for gold": A malicious explanation is that unknown writers and editors have no relationship, and the "writer" is unknown, which is not enough to "help" the editor's "busy". The "fart" of writers with status is also "fragrant"! This is also why some "Shanghai School" literati's social basis has been discovered in recent years.

Although this is a bit too harsh on the editors, it is also part of the truth. At the same time, Gao Ping Jun has let go of the editors' difficulties. We think that we don't need to blame others, let's work hard on our own!

Announcement:

For letters about literary discussions and questions similar to those raised in this article, please refer to this article and we will not answer them separately.

Western Constabulary Wins the Scott Cup: Eastern China Suffers a Crushing Defeat of Two to Zero Yesterday 180

Li Ning Injured After 15 Minutes, Ten Men Fight Hard Until the End

Western Constabulary Tall and Strong, De Fei Scores Once in Each Half

In the Scott Cup final between Eastern China and Western Constabulary, Eastern China unfortunately suffered a crushing defeat of zero to two yesterday, falling short of success. The Scott Cup was thus won by Western Constabulary. Fifteen minutes into the match, after Western Constabulary scored a goal against Eastern China, the key defender Li Ning was also injured at the same time. Li withdrew from the match from then on, and Eastern China fought hard with ten men until the end. Western Constabulary's center forward De Fei scored once in each half, making him the great hero of Western Constabulary. Yesterday, the spring weather was chilly, with drizzle coming intermittently, greatly affecting the audience, which was only about 60%, or five to six thousand people. Eastern China's crushing defeat left everyone disappointed and returning home.

How Can One Not Be Defeated Under Violence? 181

Eastern China's failure, and Li Ning's injury, was certainly one of the important reasons. Report on Inspector Hao of the Ministry of Education's Inspection of Various Sports Schools in Shanghai 186

Deeply Felt That Various Facilities Were Simple and Teachers Were Lacking

More Technical Subjects and Fewer Theoretical Subjects, Books Should Be Increased

Hao Gengsheng, Inspector of the Ministry of Education, inspected five private sports schools in Shanghai last December. The following is an excerpt from his inspection report.

One Private East Asia College of Physical Education

There are separate men's and women's departments with a total expenditure of 59,138 yuan. The total value of the school's movable and immovable property is 134,524 yuan, with an annual interest of 3,600 yuan. The school's open financial management method is still considered complete. The school buildings for the men's and women's departments occupy a total area of 19 acres and 54 square meters. There are 15 full-time teachers and 23 part-time teachers. The total number of students in the undergraduate, normal, and children's training classes is 378, including men and women. Since the school was established, a total of 872 male students and 27 female students have graduated. (Inspection Opinions) (1) The school building for the men's department is not very adequate, and the practice field is also too small. A suitable track and field stadium should be planned and constructed immediately. The school building for the women's department is a rented civilian house, which is not suitable, and the practice field is also too small. The school authorities have a plan to move the women's department to the men's department, and build a new school building for the men's department. Plans should be made quickly to ensure realization. (2) According to actual investigation, many of the school's full-time teachers also teach part-time outside. In the future, more full-time teachers should be hired as much as possible, so that they can do their best to develop school affairs. (3) In the school's total economic expenditure, salaries account for 78%, and equipment costs only account for 8%, which is too far from the ministry's equipment standards (at least 15%). Funds should be raised as soon as possible to expand equipment. (4) In terms of teaching, there are many technical subjects and fewer theoretical subjects. The curriculum distribution seems to be not very appropriate, and students should be required to bring notebooks when attending theoretical science classes, and record the materials outside of the textbooks and lectures in detail. Also, students' levels are uneven. In the future, the entrance examination should be strict when admitting new students, and the recruitment of special students should be stopped. (5) Male students eat outside the school, lacking the opportunity for communal living. The method of improvement is that students should take care of their own meals in the school. The addition of a cafeteria seems to be imminent. Also, the library equipment is too simple and should be purchased as soon as possible, and all equipment in the library should be improved, so that students have the opportunity to study automatically. (6) The school's funding is short, relying entirely on tuition fees to make up for it. In the future, funds should be raised to increase funds.

Two Private Patriotic Girls' Middle School Physical Education Department 187

The annual expenditure is 75,374 yuan, the fund has movable property of 15,086 yuan, immovable property of 102,000 yuan, and interest of 1,000 yuan. The school building area occupies 14 acres and is valued at 2,600 yuan. There are 21 full-time teachers and 8 part-time teachers. The total number of students is 228, including 29 physical education students. The school stipulates a three-year plan for the future, in terms of physical education, the first year is to enrich the physical education curriculum, and compile a physical education curriculum outline, and add a gym and softball field, etc. The second year is to expand the track and field field and plan to build a swimming pool. The third year is to improve the level of physical education and plan to set up a specialty.

(Inspection Opinions) (1) The physical education department is attached to the Patriotic Girls' School. Because the school's entire organization is still strict, the administrative organization of the physical education department is also generally complete. (2) The salaries, construction costs, and equipment costs of the physical education department are all calculated in the school's total expenses. The department's own expenditure is about 1,000 yuan per year. It is not easy to understand how it is distributed. For the convenience of statistics and for future development, the physical education department should have a separate budget and final accounts. (3) The school's entire school building was destroyed in the January 28th Incident. The school authorities were able to work hard to restore it in a short period of time and have a revitalization plan. The spirit is commendable. However, a suitable track and field field should not be lacking for a long time and should be built as soon as possible. (4) The number of students in each grade of the physical education department is too small, especially in the first and third grades. When teaching technical subjects, it is not easy to group practice due to the small number of people, and there are many difficulties. Now, the number of students should be enriched to improve the efficiency of teaching. (5) All the books in the physical education department's office should be opened in a separate room for the use of students in the physical education department, or the school's library should be expanded and a physical education library reading room should be opened separately, so that students in the physical education department have the opportunity to read freely. (6) The school's implementation of moral education is still appropriate, and student discipline is also good. Students in the physical education department should pay more attention to the implementation and management of moral education in the future, so that they can take on the responsibility of moral education within the possible scope when they teach in the future.

Three Private Southeast Women's Physical Education Normal School 188

The annual expenditure is 24,205 yuan, the fund has movable property of 20,000 yuan, and all the school buildings are newly built. There are 13 full-time teachers and 10 part-time teachers. The total number of students is 101. The school stipulates that each student must participate in an extracurricular sports activity every day, which is organized by the student union's sports department, and the teacher is only responsible for guidance and supervision. The school plans to build a swimming pool in the spring of 1934.

(Inspection Opinions) (1) Although the school's administrative organization seems simple, because the responsible personnel are always stationed at the school, they can concentrate their energy, and teachers and students are united. (2) The school has a fitness room, which seems to be sufficient for indoor classes, but the outdoor space is still too small, and it seems necessary to expand it as soon as possible. (3) The library reading area is too small and should be expanded. (4) The school's curriculum distribution is still appropriate, and students' notebook grades are also mostly commendable. However, the teachers who teach the main courses also teach the courses of another full-time teacher who leaves the school halfway. One person's energy is limited and it is difficult to complete the teaching satisfactorily. One or two more full-time teachers should be hired immediately. (5) The gymnastics teaching materials seem to be outdated and should adopt more Danish and German new teaching materials. (6) The school does not accept day students and the distribution of dormitory members is also quite appropriate. The management is quite orderly and student discipline is also good. However, in addition to sports activities, extracurricular activities such as debate meetings, concerts, academic discussion meetings, and excursions should be held regularly to adjust students' lives in school.

Four Private Liangjiang Women's Physical Education Normal School 189

Annual Expenditure: 17,160 yuan; Funds: Movable assets 40,000 yuan, Immovable assets 65,000 yuan; School buildings: Except for the rented student dormitories, the rest are self-built; Teachers: 10 full-time, 15 part-time; Students: 150 in total; Future plans: The school plans to build a three-story school building within two years, including a gymnasium, a swimming pool, and a dormitory that can accommodate 500 people. (Inspection Opinions) (1) The main staff of the school have too many concurrent teaching assignments. (2) The gym seems too small and should be expanded. The student dormitories are overcrowded and located off-campus, requiring students to cross the road to attend classes, which is very inconvenient for management. The school authorities have a plan to build a new school building and must proceed with it as soon as possible to achieve it in the short term. Also, the athletic field has not yet been built and should be added quickly. (3) In terms of teaching, technical subjects seem too heavily emphasized, while theoretical subjects are too few, which does not align well with the prescribed curriculum. Active reorganization and improvement are needed. (4) The school's student uniforms are very neat and tidy, and the students appear lively and cheerful. They hold morning exercises once a day, and the discipline is quite good. However, the average age of the first-year students is only 17, which seems too young. In the future, stricter attention should be paid to their admission qualifications when enrolling new students. (5) Because the school's dormitories are insufficient, the original library was converted into a temporary dormitory, which is a serious mistake. A separate library should be established as soon as possible for students to conduct independent research.

Five Private China Women's Physical Education Normal School 190
