Children's Weekly Spring and Autumn

About Composition 221

— Peng Xiang

Little friends: Do you know? There are four types of essays: narrative, expository, descriptive, and argumentative. Narrative and expository are relatively easy, while descriptive and argumentative are more difficult. Currently, the essay topics given by your teachers in school can be said to require you to write only the first and second types of essays mentioned above.

What is a narrative essay? A narrative essay is an essay that narrates an event. For example, writing a story or recording the work you do in a day are all this type of essay. What is an expository essay? An expository essay is an essay that explains something. For example, if your teacher gives you a topic called "Dog," you would write about what a dog looks like, what its temperament is, etc. This is an expository essay.

Descriptive and argumentative essays are not needed by you now, so I won't talk about them.

The most important thing in a narrative essay is to have order, writing down each thing in chronological order, and never making a mess of it. In an expository essay, it is necessary to have a clear understanding, to clearly recognize why this thing is different from other things, and what characteristics it has itself, etc. Little friends: If you do it according to the above method, your essays will definitely make great progress in the near future.

Wang Mian's Childhood 222

— Liu Zhongxi

At the end of the Yuan Dynasty, there appeared a strange young man named Wang Mian, who lived in a village in Zhuji County, Shaoxing Prefecture, Zhejiang Province. His father died when he was seven years old. His mother made a living by doing needlework, and the money she earned was used to support him to study in the village school. Later, because she did not have enough money to continue supporting him to study in the village school, she sent him to a neighbor's house to help them herd cattle, for which he could earn a few pennies a month. He saved the money he earned each month, and when he had free time, he would sneak into the village school to buy a few books to read. He often herded cattle by the Qiliu Lake not far from the village.

One day, he led the cattle to the side of a willow tree, and he himself lay down under the shade of the willow tree to read. Suddenly, a heavy rain passed by, and the raindrops on the lotus leaves in the lake rolled around like pearls. The blood-red sun had just emerged from the dark clouds, shining all over the lake in red. The willow trees by the lake all looked like they had been washed. The mountain streams by the lake trickled into the lake.

Seeing such a beautiful scene, he thought of the ancient saying "man in a painting." He thought, "It's a pity I can't paint, and can't paint such a beautiful scene." From then on, he was determined to learn to paint. He used his savings to buy painting supplies. Later, when he was seventeen or eighteen years old, everyone in Zhuji County knew that he was a master at painting boneless flowers.

My Mother 223

— Xue Fan

The school bell rang. I walked into the classroom. All the little brothers and sisters stood up, their dark eyes watching me.

I said: Today, everyone try to make a few short sentences. The topic is "My Mother." Each of you just needs to say a few sentences about your own mother.

The children all widened their eyes. Some smiled with their mouths open, some tilted their heads to think. They looked like they were whispering and discussing something important. Xu Jialin suddenly stood up:

"Teacher! I can do it, but I have the idea, but I can't write the sentences."

"What idea do you have?"

"I want to write: My mother only loves to play cards; but I can't write the word 'cards.'" After Xu Jialin finished speaking, all the children in the class laughed.

"Teacher! I also have an idea, but I can't write the sentences." Xue Xiaoling also stood up.

"Speak!"

"My mother has a fur coat, but I only have a small cotton-padded jacket!"

"Teacher! I have one too!" "Teacher! I want to say my idea too!" Immediately, there was a commotion in the classroom.

"Quiet! Quiet!" I pointed to the first seat in the third row. "Zhou Tiancheng, you speak first!"

The children all stared at Zhou Tiancheng with envious eyes, seeing that he had won the right to speak first.

Zhou Dacheng showed a smug smile: "When my mother has delicious chocolate candy, she always gives my younger sister more than me. What's the reason for this?"

I then asked Xu Xueshi next to Zhou Tiancheng: "Can you answer the reason Zhou Dacheng just asked?"

"I think Zhou Dacheng's mother gives her younger sister more because she is younger, is that right?"

"That's right." I replied.

I asked a few more students in turn. The children's answers were all very interesting. Because the text of this publication should not be too long, I will not write them down.

Failure and Success 224

— He Yiding

Sixth Grade, Jiangyin Private Fuyan School

In this world, no matter what you do, in the beginning, there is always "failure" and "frustration," but in the end, you will always succeed.

When I was in the first grade of Group A five years ago, I read a Chinese text whose content was: England and Scotland were at war with King Robert the Bruce. Robert the Bruce was outnumbered and defeated six times in a row. At this time, all the good generals were dead, and Robert the Bruce was lying alone in a thatched cottage in the countryside. He saw a spider spinning a web, which also failed six times, but succeeded on the seventh try. Robert the Bruce was greatly moved by this situation. He summoned his old troops again and fought England again, and thus regained Scotland. From this incident, it can be seen that for all matters, big or small, as long as you are not discouraged after failure and are willing to work hard again, you will surely succeed.

In school, we have monthly exams in each subject. After failing, we always think that we will not be able to advance to the next grade, and we become discouraged and do not study hard. This is absolutely wrong. Because we have failed, we should work harder, and not stop until we pass. This is the right thing to do.

Not only should we work hard when we fail, but we should also work hard when we pass. We must never be arrogant because we have succeeded. Then, our studies can progress even more.

Progress in Methods of Making Fire 225

— He Gongchao

From Ancient Times to the 19th Century

Among animals, only humans are able to make fire. With fire, we can cook food, light lamps, and it is not an exaggeration to say that humans have made progress compared to other animals because they obtained the method of making fire. From ancient times to the 19th century, for thousands of years, the methods humans used to make fire were initially no more than four types: "drilling," "sawing," "planing," and "striking." Later, matches appeared. The picture on the right shows the progress of these methods. (1) is the oldest method of making fire, called "hand drill." (2) is a "rope drill," which requires two people to work together. (3) is a "mouth drill." (4) is a "pump drill." The above four types all use two pieces of wood, one vertical and one horizontal, and generate heat through continuous friction, causing the shavings to burn and then fanning them into flames. (5) and (6) are both "fire-starting saws," which saw a bamboo strip sharpened into a knife edge back and forth on another bamboo strip, causing the shavings to ignite spontaneously, falling into the tinder, and then fanning them into flames. (7) is a "fire-starting plane," which planes a wooden stick back and forth in the groove of another piece of wood, gathering the shavings together. Because of the continuous friction, heat is generated, and the shavings burn. (8) is a "fire-starting gun," which has a piston inside a cylinder that moves up and down quickly. The compression of the air generates heat sufficient to ignite the tinder. (9) is pyrite and flint. (10) is a tinderbox. The above two types are both methods of making fire by "striking," striking two pieces of mineral against each other to create sparks, thereby making fire. (11) About one hundred and fifty years ago, sulfur matches were discovered, but the matches at that time had to be dipped in a burning tinderbox to produce flames. Matches that could produce fire by friction on their own, like modern matches, were not invented until 1826.

Short Jokes 226

— Li

(1) Socks

One morning, Hui'er put on the wrong socks. She wore a white sock on one foot and a black sock on the other.

So her mother told her, "Hui'er, look at yourself. You've put on the wrong socks. Hurry up and change them."

Hui'er began to stare blankly, standing there in a daze. Then she laughed loudly and immediately walked into the bedroom.

After a moment, Hui'er came out, holding the socks in her hand, and said, "Mom, how can I change them? This pair is also one black and one white!"

(2) Rainy Day

It was raining. Hui'er and Min'er were walking home from school. The two of them were walking in the heavy rain all the way.

Hui'er said, "Brother Min, hurry up. When we get home, everything will be fine. Mom is anxiously waiting for us."

Min'er said, "Sister Hui, you tell me to walk faster, but what's the use of walking faster? Isn't it still raining up ahead?"

(3) Finger

Ming'er had an extra finger on one hand. Someone said, "Ming'er, how did you get this finger?" Ming'er said, "It's made of ivory. My grandmother put it on for me." Someone said, "Well, what's the use of this finger?" Ming'er said, "It's best for picking ears!"

Number Recognition Game 227

— Yin

Children feel that arithmetic is a bit difficult. As long as they practice more, it is not difficult to overcome. As the saying goes, "practice makes perfect," which is what it means. Below, I will introduce a game to practice number recognition and fluency, to help children become proficient in mental arithmetic. During leisure time, invite a few children to play together, and it will be very interesting.

At least four people must participate in the game, and it is best if the number of people is not a multiple of three. When playing the game, everyone sits in a circle. The location of the game can be indoors or outdoors.

The method of the game is very simple. Start with anyone, and take turns counting numbers to the right: "One, two, three, four, five, six, : : :" One person counts one number, and the cycle continues. However, the person who counts the number "three" cannot say the number out loud. They can only clap on the table or the ground. For the following numbers "six," "nine," "twelve," "fifteen," : : : (all multiples of three, six, and nine), they do not need to count, but just clap their hands. For example, A counts one, B counts two, C doesn't count (claps once), D then counts four, E counts five, F doesn't count (claps once), G counts seven, H counts eight, I claps: : : This continues in a cycle. If someone who shouldn't count forgets to clap and says the number out loud, they have violated the rules. If someone who should count doesn't count and claps, it is also considered a violation of the rules. The punishment for violating the rules can be decided by the people participating in the game, but according to the results of my experiment with children, the first mistake is punished by standing up, the second violation is punished by running one lap around the outside of the game circle, and the third is punished by singing a song or telling a story. This method of punishment is more appropriate.

For younger children, you can use odd or even numbers to clap, such as clapping on even numbers or clapping on odd numbers. For older children, you can change to clapping on multiples of four, seven, : : : etc. Change as needed in application!

Weeds 228

— Jin Xi

In winter, the dew on the weeds froze into frost. The frost stung the faces of the weeds. The frost prevented the weeds from growing upwards. The weeds felt great pain.

The brave weed A roared:

"Down with the imperialist frost! Drive away the evil frost!"

Countless weeds also learned to shout loudly.

Weed B inserted a cold question:

"What power can we use to defeat the frost?"

The weeds shouting slogans were silent.

Weed B then offered an opinion: "Under the oppression of the frost's violence, our only solution is to endure humiliation and seek revenge. We will put all our nutrients into our roots to strengthen our strength. When spring comes, we will seize the opportunity to drive away the frost and fight for our freedom. Shouting slogans is in vain. This is our revenge plan."

The weeds listened. The leaves turned yellow. The nutrients in the leaves were all put into the roots. They were all preparing to endure humiliation and seek revenge.

Dog Jokes 229

— Ou

It is said that this year is the "Year of the Dog," and the children born this year should belong to the dog sign.

In a certain school, a student surnamed Zhang, who is twelve years old this year, is very gluttonous. When eating at the same table, he always eats more than his share. Everyone at the table dislikes him very much.

Once, there was a dinner party. Zhang ate greedily, reverting to his old habits. Li, who was sitting at the same table, knew that he belonged to the dog sign. He deliberately asked him, "May I ask what your honorable age belongs to?"

"Dog," Zhang replied.

"That's good," Li continued, "If you belonged to the tiger, everyone at our table would be eaten by you."

Zhang's face turned red with shame after hearing this.

Having Hands and Feet 230

— Shi Yusheng

Dad asked me what kind of person I wanted to be. "Someone with hands and feet!" I replied. "Silly child! Who doesn't have hands and feet!" Dad laughed.

"Yes, everyone has hands and feet," I said. "But, if you have hands and don't use them, and have feet and don't move them, won't you become a useless person who has no hands or feet? We are born with two hands to use, and we are born with two feet to move. I want to use my hands to do what I should do; I want to move my feet to walk the path I should walk—until my blood runs dry and my limbs wither!"

"My good child! : : :" A smile appeared in the corner of Dad's eyes, and a right hand that had tasted the bitterness of the world was messing up my hair.

Tomorrow is "Arbor Day"! Little friends! Go afforest with your teachers or parents. If you want to understand the benefits of afforestation, you can ask your teacher.

Monkey Show 231

— Shou Cheng

"Tang, tang"! A monkey show is being performed on the northeast open ground of the Hua family. Beating the gong, beating the drum, the monkey showman holds the iron chain of the performing monkey in one hand, and dances the whip in the other, leading the monkey from east to west, here to there, singing loudly in his mouth:

"The performance is a set, the monkey wears a top hat for the show."

The monkey actually puts on a red-tasseled hat, jumping and scurrying, causing a slight laugh from the surrounding audience.

He makes the monkey play tricks such as riding on the back of a sheep, jumping through iron hoops, somersaulting, and climbing high poles. Although the monkey is very unwilling in its heart, when it sees the whip in his hand, it dares not disobey. Finally, the monkey is mechanically led back to the corner of the ground, and the broken box is opened. The monkey showman sings loudly again:

"The tricks are new again, seeing the monkey wearing a dragon robe"!

A spectator impatiently said: "Isn't this the old trick that was played on the wasteland of the Han family on the banks of the Yalu River before? What's the point of watching it?"

(A critique of Puyi's desire to usurp the throne and proclaim himself emperor.)

To the Little Warriors 232

— Xu Zongjie

Little friends, you are as happy as little angels; you are as gentle as white lambs. But behind you, there are demons with smiling faces, tempting you to fall. Ahead of you, there are venomous snakes and fierce beasts entrenched, preventing your progress. Little friends; quickly put on the armor of perseverance; quickly wield the sword of wisdom, cut a glorious path, walk and walk, until you reach the peak of victory. Warriors! Our little warriors! You must cultivate the spirit of great fearlessness; supplement it with sufficient knowledge; and also have the instinct for unity and cooperation. Only in this way can you become an all-powerful warrior; only in this way can you be a victorious warrior who "conquers every battle and overcomes every attack." Little friends! I now congratulate you in advance, celebrating your future success.

Flour Marked by Recent and Distant Gains 248

Yesterday in the flour market, after the opening bell in the morning, all months showed an upward trend. With quotations from abroad, Chicago rose by four cents and Canada by about ten cents, so after the opening prices were announced, sentiment was already stable. Furthermore, although the government wheat had been entirely sold off, it was heard that various factories, due to special relationships, unanimously adhered to a policy of not selling, which made the market atmosphere more firm. It was thought that since the factories were not selling, the market could at least hold steady for a while, so short covering and speculative longs also bought in, and the market atmosphere felt good. By the afternoon opening, the market atmosphere continued to improve. The current month rose an additional cent due to northern buyers, while the forward months rose because of short covering and purchases by domestic factories, in addition to the morning gains. Based on the current trend, since the factories have made prior commitments, they are not likely to change their attitude for the time being, so temporary stability is expected. As a result, the current month rose two and a half cents compared to the previous day, April/May rose two cents, June rose two and a half cents, July rose two and seven and a half tenths of a cent, and August rose two and a half cents.

Fishing: Japanese Fishing Vessels Frequently Arrive 251

Small Yellow Croaker is the Mainstay

Recently, the encroachment of Japanese fishing vessels has become active again. Last month, the Japanese fishing vessel Man** Maru arrived, causing turmoil in the fish market. Unexpectedly, that same Man** Maru arrived again the day before yesterday (the 8th), with approximately 724 boxes of illegally caught fish, mostly small yellow croaker, weighing about 130 dan, with a total sales price of over $2,400. Yesterday (the 9th), the fishing vessel Daxin Maru also arrived, with a total catch of 800 boxes, also mostly small yellow croaker, with a total sales price of over $3,000. It is said that these fish are unloaded at the China Merchants Wharf at the 16th Pier and sold by Shenfeng and four other fish firms on consignment. As a result of this dumping of Japanese fish, domestic fishing vessels and the fresh fish industry are suffering huge losses. Even foreign ships arriving on the same day are said to have lost over $500 as a result.

Silk and Tea: Listless Silk Trade 252

||Export of Ji'li Silk Reduces by Half||

Every year, my country's Ji'li silk exports around 20,000 bales to Europe and the United States. In recent years, due to the encroachment of Japanese silk and poor reeling quality, exports have gradually decreased. From June 1st of last year to the end of February this year, Ji'li silk exports totaled only 2,373 bales. In the same period last year, a total of 4,741 bales were exported, a reduction of five-tenths.

Recently, due to the restoration of the upper Yangtze River shipping, Chuanhuang coarse silk is being transported to Shanghai in a steady stream. Yesterday, Bao Taihe Yellow Silk Store also received 26 pieces of Jinzhou yellow silk for sale in the store.

In the overseas raw silk market, sales of Chinese silk factories remain sluggish, and market prices are weak. The Shanghai port telegraph transfers are silent, and telegrams for yellow and white silk are rarely sent out. The future is again in a dire situation. Yesterday, only the Shanghai Silk Factory purchased ten bales of white factory silk, and Xinfu purchased ten bales of Sichuan yellow factory silk, with prices trending downwards.

Piece Goods: Sample Business of Woolen Fabrics Sharply Increases 253

The woolen fabric industry has always been divided into the Western-style clothing and the general clothing categories. Western-style materials often come with samples that are distributed to tailors, commonly known as the "Hongkou gang" sample shops. For many years, the general woolen fabric trade has been concentrated in the Qipanjie area, with shops selling single-width fabrics for Chinese-style clothing, marked with sizes and prices, for customers to browse and choose. The sample shops do not sell single-width fabrics, as they specialize in selling to Western-style tailors. Recently, with the arrival of the warm spring season, there has been a sudden increase in orders for Western-style clothing, which has led to a sharp increase in the sample business of these sample shops, especially in the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou railway areas, where purchases are most frequent.

Ribbed steel bars are currently selling for $109, which is slightly lower than before, but sales to customers have been developing. In recent days, over 120 tons have been sold. Transactions by local construction firms are normal. It is heard that there have not been many arrivals in recent days, so there is little expectation of change in the future.

Company Iron Fixed Price Reported Rise 255

It is heard that there are no futures contracts available for the next month, so the Shanghai market is exceptionally strong, and factory demand has increased sharply. It is found that 1,400 to 1,500 boxes have been transacted in recent days. Old steel factory goods are selling for $28.50, and new steel factory goods are selling for $28. It is heard that the inventory is extremely low, and there are few arrivals, so the market atmosphere is exceptionally solid.

Women's Corner, Issue 4

Two Pressing Issues for Modern Women 276

— Bi Yun

| Freedom of Marriage and Freedom of Occupation | I don't think anyone can deny that the most pressing and difficult issues for modern young people, both male and female, are marriage and occupation. These two issues, while seemingly "old hat," are in fact increasingly important in human life. We only need to pay a little attention to the essays in newspapers and magazines depicting the pain and boredom of young people, and the frequent news of their suicides. If we trace the causes, it is either the pressure of life or the lack of freedom in marriage or broken love. Especially for women, the pain and oppression of these two issues in today's society are even more severe.

Let's start with marriage. "Freedom of marriage" naturally refers to marriage based on love. The words "love" are so fragrant, beautiful, and tender! The ecstatic "youthful love" is a supreme and beautiful art, a fundamental desire of every young man and woman, a natural voice from the depths of the human soul. But in this society where everything is commodified, such love-based marriages are rare. Because in this mercenary society, all issues revolve around money, and therefore the decision of relationships between the sexes is based on money, not love. People without money will not be loved. A very lively and beautiful young man, if he doesn't have the ability to support a wife, is often a loser in the field of love. It's the same for women. Those modern ladies in high society have money and time to go to dance halls, universities, and other entertainment venues, and have access to men, so they can fully enjoy the joy of being in love. Women in the middle class rarely have this opportunity. As for the countless working women in cities and the poor girls in the countryside, they often become prostitutes due to the pressure of life, and are forced to live a life of prostitution, satisfying the lust of all the men they don't want. This is their freedom. So, in today's society, so-called freedom of marriage is just a patent for the leisure class! Strictly speaking, it is only the freedom to exchange money and cosmetics!

As for women's occupations, although various sectors of society have opened up many avenues for women to earn a living, from government agencies to banks, post offices, telephones, and stores, they all employ female staff, but this can only accommodate a small number of women with relatively high social status and specialized skills. The most common occupations are working in factories and being elementary school teachers. Those who are elementary school teachers also live in a state of competition, panic, and instability. Those who are teachers in public schools often don't receive their salaries and experience financial panic. Those who are teachers in private schools are treated exceptionally poorly. An elementary school teacher works non-stop all day long and only earns ten to thirty yuan a month at most. As for the working women who work in factories, their miserable lives are even more unspeakable. They work twelve hours a day doing mechanical work in smoky, noisy factories, and the wages they earn are not enough to maintain even the minimum standard of living. Therefore, those female workers who cannot maintain their lives, and those women who simply cannot find work, are ultimately forced to become prostitutes, which is the most lowly free occupation for women. From this point of view, the so-called freedom of occupation for women, under the current social conditions, cannot be universally obtained by women, and even those who have already obtained it will only face another layer of oppression!

From this, it can be seen that the issue of marriage and occupation is not a simple and isolated issue, but is closely related to the entire society. However, due to the limited space of this article, I cannot fully elaborate on my personal views on this issue. I sincerely hope that male and female friends who are enthusiastic about women's issues will actively participate in the discussion and offer criticisms and corrections to this article.

The Issue of Private Prostitution 277

— Tong Hua

For the sake of international reputation, the Beijing authorities abolished public prostitution several years ago. However, while public prostitution was abolished, private prostitution is thriving. A special dispatch from Beijing in the Shen Bao on the 5th of this month stated:

"Private prostitution is rampant in Beijing, and according to a survey, there are as many as 3,000 prostitutes. Since the beginning of spring, the number of venereal disease patients in the Central Hospital has exceeded 100 per day, which is ten times more than any other disease. The situation is the same in the Gulou Hospital. Moreover, the number is increasing year by year, which is worrying."

The seriousness of the private prostitution issue lies not only in the annual increase in venereal diseases, but also in the large-scale collapse of the rural economy. Imperialism and feudal forces are destroying the Chinese countryside with a two-pronged approach, and the man-made natural disasters have exacerbated the bankruptcy of the rural economy. Water plants, leaves, tree bark, wheat seedlings, and Guanyin clay have become the food of farmers, and selling children has become their way to alleviate their plight. In Shaanxi, orphaned girls in their teens are sold for one or two yuan, but there are few takers. In the Quanzhou area of Zhejiang, a thirteen-year-old girl can be indentured for five years for only six yuan, and an eight-year-old girl can be sold for only twenty-two yuan, including the middleman's fee. Even a ten-year-old girl can only be sold for fifty yuan. In Guangdong, due to the collapse of the silk industry and the closure of silk factories, more than 200,000 female workers have lost their jobs. In order to survive, they have to flock to Guangzhou to work as maids or engage in secret prostitution. From the Northwest to the Southeast, where is it not a living hell? Nanjing, which once had the reputation of "golden powder" in history, is naturally no exception. We can vividly imagine what Jiangnan is like now by looking at the rice riots in Wuxi, the disturbances in Yangzhou, the decline of commerce in Suzhou, and the heavy taxes in Jiangning (the land tax is about one yuan per mu, accounting for a quarter of the annual harvest of the entire mu). Selling children is inevitable, and the increase in the number of women falling into the fire pit is inevitable.

At the same time, on the other hand, there is a need for the existence of prostitutes. As the capital, scholars seeking official positions and imposing military generals naturally flock here. These people, even though they have young wives at home who "regret teaching their husbands to seek titles," are far from home, and while embracing others, they are also moved by the beauty of Jinling, and naturally want to visit brothels. Under these circumstances, supply meets demand, and business is bound to flourish. The talk of benevolence and morality cannot withstand the scourging of life. Thus, the capital, on the surface, does not allow public prostitution, but private prostitution has finally become a matter of public knowledge.

The Beijing authorities have long known the truth of the matter and once advocated lifting the ban last year. For the sake of revenue and the fact that it has become an open secret, the authorities' move can be called straightforward. However, the Women's Association, in order to protect women's rights, rose up to oppose it and put forward the following relief measures:

(1) Representatives from party, government, military, police, and women's organizations should inspect daily. If private prostitutes are found, they should be taken into the relief home for accommodation.

(2) The government should expand the existing women's education and training centers in the relief home to serve as accommodation and relief centers.

(3) The party, government, military, police, and women's organizations should jointly establish a large-scale women's factory to accommodate them and teach them various crafts.

These measures, while seemingly reasonable on the surface, are actually scratching the surface. Under the dumping of goods by imperialism, factories in Shanghai and Tianjin are reducing their workforce or closing down. The original female workers have become unemployed. How can new large-scale women's factories be established? Under the total bankruptcy of the national economy, the surplus population is increasing day by day. Even if the education and training centers in various places are expanded, how can they accommodate this huge number of people? Moreover, the government is currently facing a financial deficit. How can these measures be realized?

The prostitution system is an inevitable phenomenon in the current society. Public and private prostitution are essentially the same. The only difference is whether it is recognized in law or not. Only by eliminating the fundamental contradictions of the current society can the prostitution system be eliminated. People fighting for women's rights! Grasp the center of the problem! Abandoning the root and pursuing the tip will only be in vain.

National Goods Women's Day 278

— Yao

Women's Day falls on China, quietly like white feathers floating on still water. Fortunately, there are a few women's associations that held joint gatherings: performing entertainment, promoting national goods, etc., which can be considered enlightened women in China, not falling behind international women.

In fact, in these years, full of wounds and wandering, after examining the internal and external situation, if we want to talk about making money for the public and private, the best thing is to promote national goods. We women, promoting national goods to save the country, even if we don't hold anything in common with international women on today's "March 8th," it's not necessarily a bad thing. However, it just so happens that "March 8th" Women's Day is also a national good. We should not be indifferent. Unfortunately, most people ignore it, thinking it is an imported product, afraid of causing trouble and remain silent. So today, it is so silent everywhere, it is really wrong! I am not as stubborn as Master Kang, advocating that the radio was also invented by Confucius; but "celebrating March 8th" is indeed a quintessence of women's philosophy, and now let's give a superficial lecture.

What is "March 8th"?

First, it is the eight characters, the year, month, day, and hour of a woman's birth, her eight characters. Once she enters someone else's door, she has gained "the one to rely on." So, marry a chicken and follow the chicken, marry a dog and follow the dog, and there is no need to have a wandering mind for life.

Second, it is the eight obediences. On top of obeying her father, husband, and son, she must also obey fate, the blue sky, the powerful, Yuan Shikai, and cars. There is no need to work hard to be independent.

Third, it is the eight segments. The head, chest, abdomen, hips, two hands, and two legs, these eight segments of the body, are exhibited for people to judge. Then her food, clothing, shelter, and transportation will naturally be what she wants, and she will be outstanding. There is no need to rely on vigorous movements to protect her.

The above-mentioned domestic women's "March 8th" does not contain any foreign goods. In this year of national goods, we can frankly and loudly call for it. And on this Women's Day of national goods, we can widely promote national goods, so that powerless women can also participate in the great cause of saving the country, and practice the skills of bearing heavy responsibilities and going far. This brings unlimited glory to the future of women.

As for the Women's Day of foreign goods, it contains ominous fighting characteristics: demanding what equality, what liberation, what raising the status of women, what improving the treatment of working women, etc., which may be said to be out of touch with the times for us. It is better to promote national goods and resist foreign goods. In the country, we cooperate and work together. When men are busy eliminating internal chaos and resisting for a long time, women work hard to promote the sale of national goods and economic construction. We fulfill our responsibility as a member of the public, and contribute to the national goods women's movement for ourselves.

Therefore, although there are commemorative days on the eighth, such as September 18th, January 28th, etc., for us, only this year's "March 8th" of the Women's National Goods Year is the most meaningful.

The Soviet Union's Five-Year Plan and Women 279

— [blank]

(1) Women's Efforts for the Five-Year Plan: The success of the Soviet Union's Five-Year Plan has become an obvious fact.

However, its success is by no means like many other historical events, completed by men alone. In the process of the Five-Year Plan's victory, Soviet women have indeed shown a very important position. In the Soviet Union, all women who participate in production, whether they are urban workers or rural farmers, understand the tasks and significance of the Five-Year Plan. They feel the responsibility they should bear for all constructions, and they are moving forward vigorously.

At the beginning of the Five-Year Plan, everyone was working hard to achieve the following goals:

(1) Who can relatively reduce the cost of production,

(2) Who can produce the best things,

(3) Who is working hard not to let the machine space. This competitive attitude expanded from individual workers to each other, between male and female workers, between workers and farmers, to each factory, each industrial sector, each city, and each rural area. In this competition, working women have done amazing work. For example, a working woman who usually could only produce 720 pieces a day, produced 954 pieces on the first day of the competition, and increased it to 1,020 pieces the next day.

The treatment they receive in their work is exactly the same as that of men. In the same labor, men and women receive the same wages, and there is no difference in terms of law.

(2) Progress of Women's Education: In the process of implementing the Five-Year Plan, Soviet women were able to undertake this great task, obviously they must have considerable knowledge and technical ability. However, in the Soviet Union, there were few people with education and technical ability, especially women. Therefore, at the beginning of the Five-Year Plan, the first thing to do was to overcome this shortcoming, especially the elimination of illiteracy. From 1927 to 1928, people in the Soviet Union who could read and write accounted for 53.9% of the total population. By 1932, the end of the Five-Year Plan, 82% of illiteracy had been overcome.

Of course, being able to read is not enough, so after Soviet women achieved the goal of being able to read and write, they further demanded to acquire specialized knowledge, in order to be able to work in factory management or agricultural management, and to engage in guidance. In 1929, there were 8,818 women studying in various industrial or agricultural specialized schools in the Soviet Union, of which 20% were working women. There were 4,784 women studying in industrial schools, of which 83% were working women. There were 4,975 women in vocational schools, of which 47% were the children of workers. There were 7,079 girls in factory-affiliated schools, of which 84% were the daughters of workers. Rural women have also made significant progress. In 1929, 21% of the students in Soviet higher education institutions were women who had previously engaged in agriculture or worked in their hometowns. Other labor specialized schools had 32% rural girls, technical schools had 20%, and various agricultural training schools also had 27%.

(3) Liberation of Family Life: In the process of rapid industrialization in the Soviet Union, working women, because they participated in this new type of production, of course there would be huge changes in their daily lives. This change is the new liberation that the Five-Year Plan bestowed on Soviet women. The first is to be freed from the pain of spending all their time raising children. In the Five-Year Plan, many nurseries were set up in all newly established labor areas, and near factories and workers' residences in cities. Many kindergartens and playgrounds were also set up in residential cooperatives or large residences for the purpose of accommodating children.

To reduce the burden on rural women, there are similar facilities in collective farms. All larger collective farms had more than a thousand nurseries by the end of the fifth year. In the nurseries, someone is taking care of the children diligently, and knowledgeable teachers are paying attention to the children's education. Everything in life is regular and appropriate, so that mothers working in factories can rest assured. There are also children's sections in the clubs, so that when mothers bring their children to the club, they will not be disturbed by the children and hinder their own rest and entertainment.

Of equal importance to the liberation of raising children is the establishment of many public kitchens. Many of these public kitchens are large kitchen factories equipped with modern technology. These kitchen factories are equipped with extremely clean and satisfactory dining rooms. At the end of the fifth year, there were 4,800 large kitchen factories, supplying meals to 20 million people.

All of these facilities, whether nurseries, kindergartens, children's sections, or public canteens, as well as public laundries, are all aimed at transferring the troubles of housework to society, so that women can be liberated from unproductive labor, engage in productive labor, and enter reading clubs to satisfy their burning desire to be educated.

In short, the success of the Soviet Union's Five-Year Plan is gradually liberating women from their historical inhuman lives and introducing them to the realm of freedom and equality.

Women in Rural Nantong 280

— Zi Ming

If we want to understand the level of evolution of the people in a particular place, we can determine it by their lifestyle. Recently, there has been considerable attention in the country to the customs and habits of various regions. Even remote villages in the mountains and valleys are explored using every possible means. Perhaps this is not just a matter of impulsive interest, but a question concerning the future of the entire nation?

Nantong is known as a model county, with highly developed industry and commerce, hence the name "Shanghai of Jiangbei." However, what is their lifestyle like? Especially the women's? The women of the city will be described in another article. Now, I will first present various aspects of the women in rural Nantong below.

The women in rural Nantong are completely dominated by their environment. They have their own unique environment, which shapes their unique behaviors. What is their environment? "Bandits are numerous as hairs, the people have no means of living!" Coupled with their adherence to tradition, this forms their special way of life.

Habits: They are generally honest and simple, with peaceful temperaments. They dislike traveling far, are attached to their hometown, preferring a life of dullness rather than seeking development. Their vision is narrow, they perceive the world as too vast. Originally, crossing the Yangtze River shouldn't be a big deal, but they think, "A pregnant woman crossing the river is perilous!" Therefore, they only have "home" in their minds. They don't know what the nation and society are. They are very fond of their relatives.

Dress: Their dress is completely in the national style. They worship "three-inch golden lotuses." Every girl must bind her feet. Their feet are practically two bamboo sticks. When they walk, they sway and tilt, like toddlers learning to walk. Their clothing is very simple, made from cotton seeds to cotton, cotton yarn, and cotton cloth, all made directly by themselves without relying on external forces.

Marriage: Women never openly discuss matters between men and women. They are entirely controlled by "the orders of parents and the words of matchmakers." If they marry a good husband, they say their parents have foresight. If not, it is their predetermined fate. Everyone believes that "marriages are made three thousand years ago." If they are dissatisfied with their marriage, you won't hear it from their mouths. Even having such a thought is a sin. So, when a husband unfortunately dies young, they must sacrifice their youth and remain a widow. The same goes for those who are not yet married. There are also many marriages that are arranged before they are even born.

Beliefs: They are very religious, worshipping idols. Among all the gods, Guanyin Bodhisattva is the central object of devotion. Every year on the 19th day of the second, sixth, and tenth lunar months, gatherings are held. Women of all ages fast beforehand. On these days, they burn incense and candles, and kneel in worship, with hundreds of people gathering in groups. In addition to worship, they also murmur the Guanyin Sutra. --Seeking elixirs! Praying for children! Asking for fortunes! : : : Many problems that cannot be solved in ordinary times are brought to Guanyin for guidance.

Because Nantong has been plagued by bandits for several years, many innocent people have been killed by them. Fortunately, the banditry has calmed down somewhat, but the so-called government troops and defense corps still rob and kill as usual. This deep impression lingers in their minds. They see through life and death, considering them nothing. Thus, everyone tends to be more passive, believing in Buddhism, reciting "Namo Amitabha" morning and night, hoping that after suffering in this world, they can go to the Western Paradise to enjoy bliss, or be reborn into a good family.

Work: Women absolutely manage all household affairs. Cooking and laundry are their compulsory subjects, as well as household arrangement, and sewing for their children: : : all are their duties. In addition to doing housework, they also work in the fields, helping the men.

Status: They absolutely obey their husbands. However, there is no so-called suppression on the husband's part. There is also a phenomenon where husbands obey their wives in household matters, while wives obey their husbands in matters outside the household. This is a method of division of labor and cooperation.

As for finances, they are entirely in the hands of men. They have no possibility of participating in social affairs.

Due to limited space, the details of the rural women in Nantong must be left at this point. After reading this, readers will definitely doubt the name of the model county, right? --The division between city and countryside lies here.

Questions and Answers on Women's Diseases

(I) Letter 281

To the esteemed editor of the Women's Garden section of the February 18th issue, in "A Woman's Life," there is a section on children suffering from pinworms. My household has a girl who is six years old and quite healthy. Every evening, she cries out that her anus is in pain, which I suspect is due to this strange ailment. This has been going on for about four months. More than a month ago, I went to Wuzhou Pharmacy and bought a bottle of Jianji Candy. After eating several pieces, a worm like a chopstick was excreted, but recently the anal pain has greatly reduced. I went to the hospital for a diagnosis, but they couldn't find anything wrong, and it cannot be completely cured. If you have a good remedy, please advise and I will be grateful. Respectfully, and wishing the editor of the Women's Garden section good health.

(II) Reply from Medical Consultant Chen Fang 282

— Lan Bishan

A worm like a chopstick excreted after taking Jianji Candy is a roundworm, not a pinworm. Adult pinworms usually live in the rectum. If you want to get rid of them, Jianji Candy can be used. However, the worms are small, and ordinary people often don't pay attention and cannot find them in the stool. The letter says, "The child cries out that her anus is in pain, which I suspect is itchy." But that's just a guess. Whether it's caused by pinworms is still a question. To determine if she has pinworms, you only need to use a microscope to check her stool for worm eggs, which is very easy. To determine whether her anus is in pain or itchy, there should also be a method, but I can only give a clear answer after an examination.

A Woman's Life 283

— Xuan Wen

Three, The Age of Yearning

After a girl's first menstruation, great changes occur in her body. The first menstruation is a symbol of the completion of a girl's reproductive system.

When a girl reaches this period, her skin gradually becomes soft, her hair shiny, her cheeks flushed, and her whole body becomes exceptionally rich and beautiful. This is all caused by the endocrine secretions circulating in the body from the reproductive glands.

At this time, not only do changes occur in a girl's body, but there are also unusual signs in her emotions.

During this period, she often gazes at her own image in the mirror, which is the first step towards heterosexual love. She gazes at her own image in the mirror as if it were the object of her love. But she unconsciously seeks a real object of love.

A certain Western painter once painted a picture of a girl kissing her own image in the mirror, which clearly symbolizes a kind of love consciousness and immediately evokes feelings of love. This impulse to love oneself is called the Narcissus phenomenon, named after the story of the beautiful youth Narcissus in ancient Greek mythology who fell in love with his own reflection in the water.

The rising demand for love in a girl's blood cannot be satisfied with her own image in the mirror, so she turns to love of the same or opposite sex. Homosexual love is more likely to occur in factories or school dormitories. This is a pathological condition, and if properly guided, it can enhance a girl's emotions and cultivate her appreciation of beauty. Conversely, it can be quite harmful. As a result of homosexual love, she may not be able to marry a healthy person of the opposite sex, or she may dislike marriage and live a life of perverted love. There are also cases where it disappears naturally after having a lover or getting married. This kind of perverted life and love is harmful and useless. It is necessary for parents and teachers to advise and guide them well.

Shen Bao Amateur Weekly

Amateur Talk

A Word to My Fellow Amateur Students 284

— Gong Pu

Everyone feels depressed these days, and most people don't have a way to relieve their depression. Is it impossible to relieve depression? That may not be the case. Although it's really not easy to solve depression before society stabilizes, if we can thoroughly understand the future direction of society and think about how individuals should adapt to the current society, it's not absolutely impossible to find a solution. Because depression arises from our lack of ways to adapt to the environment. If we have a way, depression can be reduced. Reading is one way we currently think can solve this depression, because although we can feel the state of our environment in daily life, it is unsystematic, trivial, vague, and obscure. If we can further use scientific methods to study the causal laws of objective phenomena, we will be able to understand the environment very thoroughly and clearly. So what we mean by reading is not rote memorization, but using a scientific spirit to study reality. Our purpose in reading is not to kill time, let alone to have others praise us, but to enable us to adapt to or transform the environment, rather than being bound and dominated by the environment.

This article is aimed at general amateur students. The above paragraph is written with this in mind, because I have recently been working at an amateur school and have found that at the beginning of the semester, there are a lot of people in each class, usually five or sixty people in each class, but later the number slowly decreases. By the end of the semester, there are often only twenty or thirty people, or even ten or so people left. This situation is especially common in foreign language classes. I am very surprised by this situation. Why do they drop out halfway? Later, after our investigation and repeated conversations with them, we learned that there are roughly three reasons why they drop out halfway:

(1) The teacher's teaching method is not good;

(2) The readers are all employed, and due to fatigue or busyness in their spare time, they often have to miss classes. Later, because they missed too many classes, they couldn't catch up, so they simply stopped reading;

(3) At first, they had a high interest and desire to read, but after reading for a few weeks or two months, they felt that reading was not an easy task and that it required a considerable amount of time to be effective, so they became discouraged and stopped reading. Looking at the above three reasons, in addition to the first one, which is not a problem and should be the responsibility of the school (such as the schools run by our organization now, our teachers are either successful in the past or are hired after careful consideration), the second and third items are not shortcomings in our teaching, but that readers do not have a thorough understanding of reading, so they lack perseverance and laziness. Therefore, I briefly discussed the "purpose of reading" above, hoping that readers will increase their courage to read. However, this cannot be discussed in detail here. Please refer to the previous "Reading Questions and Answers" in this newspaper, which has a more detailed discussion. (Such as "On Self-Study" on January 6th and 7th; "The Fundamental Problems of Reading" on January 27th, 28th, and 29th; "The Seriousness of Reading" on February 3rd, etc.)

We know that we all have a kind of inertia. We often decide to do something, and we also know that it is worthwhile and must be done, but later we often procrastinate and become lazy, putting that thing aside. This is a common problem of people and is not surprising, but if we can use reason and determination in everything we do, it is not impossible to overcome. So the first thing to do is not to be afraid of difficulties and not to be lazy. But while this is the most important point in doing things, objective difficulties can often affect the courage to do things. For example, if "missing a few classes makes it impossible to catch up later," then it is not a matter of determination to do things, but a problem of learning difficulties in fact. Therefore, after discussion, we want to try a method for this: we hope that the students in each class will organize a mutual aid reading group based on the spirit of mutual assistance. The method is for everyone to publicly choose a student with excellent grades and who is willing to serve everyone to help. Students who miss classes can ask them for help with the missed lessons and for help with things they don't understand. Because the teacher should be responsible for answering questions about academic matters, but the difficulties caused by missing classes should not be asked in class, which wastes the time of the whole class. If this method of mutual assistance is used, we deeply feel that those who are helped will certainly benefit a lot, but those who help can also take this opportunity to deepen the impression of the knowledge they have already acquired. Moreover, we know that sometimes we think we understand everything when we read, but when others question us, we become confused again. This often happens, so those who help can take this opportunity to check their reading and strive to achieve the purpose of teaching and learning from each other. In short, we think this method is very important and very beneficial, so we specifically propose it for discussion, for the reference of amateur students and those engaged in amateur education.

Life

The Disasters of Sexual Desire 285

— Nu Lu

The ancients said: "Food and sex are human nature." And: "Food and sex, the great desires of man, exist." Thank God! Not only did he create man, but he also created "sex": not only did he make people think of food when hungry and drink when thirsty, but he also made people aware of youth and beauty and experience sexual hunger and thirst when they reach a certain age. What makes people especially grateful is that God's rewards and punishments are clear, and his grace and power are both present. They are all God's children, but he allows some to obtain the highest degree of satisfaction of food and sex without labor, while others have to work hard, live frugally, and excessively restrain sexual desire and reproduction. Some people are even forced to sell their "sex" in exchange for "food." This is probably because the former are the favored children of heaven, who should receive heavenly gifts; the latter are deeply sinful and should be condemned by heaven!

Now let's put aside the problem of "food" and only talk about my personal "sex" life over the past year.

Many people regard "sex" as an obscene matter. Therefore, in order to avoid the suspicion of "pandering to lust," I have tried my best to use a solemn tone when writing this article.

My wife and I are both salaried workers; my monthly salary is twenty yuan, and my wife can earn fifteen yuan per month. But we both have to take care of our own food and lodging. And there is no fixed property at home, so life can only barely get by. What is barely satisfactory is that we have been married for a year and still don't have a child, which is what we often consider to be fortunate.

My wife is a strange person. Like some women, she doesn't want to have children. She even gets anxious and upset when she hears other people's children crying. I have never seen her hug or kiss anyone's child. She doesn't like to do this, nor does she need to. In her mind, it seems that only "working" and "making money" are what she often thinks about. The tempering of life has gradually disappeared her innate motherhood!

As for me? I don't want to have children either. However, it's not that I don't want to have children, it's just that the environment doesn't allow me to have them, so I have to use all kinds of methods to excessively restrain sexual desire and reproduction.

I have thought about it this way: if my wife becomes pregnant and has a child, then she will not be able to work for at least two months. In this way, even if she doesn't resign from the company, the company will fire her. It is obviously impossible to get their permission to find someone to replace her or take a long vacation. She will only lose her job. You must know that life is a serious matter. Once she loses her job, it will be difficult to find another job after she recovers. Moreover, children need to be cared for and raised. Whether you pay to hire a nanny or the mother abandons her career to pursue "good mother and virtuous wife-ism," you will always have to add a large burden to your life and sacrifice a portion of your limited income. In this way, the so-called "little angel," once viewed through the eyes of us poor people, will immediately turn into a debt-collecting "living ghost." Just one of these "living ghosts" is enough to kill us, let alone hoping for "many sons and grandsons" and "a house full of children!"

Children are a disaster, sexual desire is the root of this disaster, and "poverty" is the root of the root of this disaster. On our first night of marriage, the terror of this disaster threatened us jealously, but fortunately, no evil was sown that night. Later, we adopted a separate bed system and paid attention to texts on contraception in newspapers and magazines.

I don't know which newspaper I saw a piece of information saying that from the sixteenth day after the start of the previous menstruation to the start of the next menstruation, a total of thirteen days is the period of non-conception, and the risk is the least during this period. We adopted this method.

In fact, even during the so-called "non-conception period," we only dare to sleep together once a month at most, and we don't dare to be too unrestrained, lest we sow an evil seed. No wonder my wife once said to me like this:

"I don't know why, but I always feel like you are not my own man, but like I stole you."

My wife is right. A poor woman with a poor husband is the same as having none. Fortunately, we are not "well-fed," so we don't often "think of lust." The fatigue of working every day suppresses our physiological needs!

Although I am always so careful every time, in fact, I still can't relax. Every time I always suspect: "Will this time sow an evil seed? Is it really impossible to conceive during the non-conception period?" I worry and fret all day long, and unease occupies my whole heart, and I don't even have the energy to work. One act of indulgence is not worth the loss of ten or twenty days of worry and anxiety!

In the evening, when I come home from the company and meet my wife coming back, I often have to ask her like this: "Has your period come?" If the answer is "not yet," then I suspect even more: "Maybe the period hasn't arrived yet? Or has an evil seed been sown?" I am anxious and fretful, and my heart is even more uneasy. It seems that I have already seen the fetus wriggling in her belly, and the matter is even more serious. In this way, I always have to wait until one day she tells me: "It's here!" before I can completely relax.

Thank God! I still don't have a child. I hope I won't have one in the future. Under the current social system, for the sake of life, I would rather be an unfilial person who is "childless is the greatest filial impiety!"

A Spring-Filled Evening in a Room 286

— Da Ke

A big guy with a fierce face and a bamboo stick in his hand ordered him to untie his belt and socks and throw them on the ground. After searching him all over, he pushed him into the prison door, which was as thick as a lettuce bowl, and locked the door with a clang.

"Old Yu! Why are you here too?" Xiao Chen got up from the ground and asked with a bitter smile.

He glanced at Xiao Chen, gently replied to Xiao Chen, "How long have you been here?" and sat down in a corner directly opposite the toilet, holding his head in his hands and crouching on his knees, without saying a word.

"Dinner is served. Don't be anxious, new comrade. Eat something first." Hemp-faced A San approached him and said, while handing him a tin rice bowl and a pair of chopsticks.

He ignored him. He was thinking silently about when he left home today, his wife was holding the two-month-old child and lying on the bed, singing a monotonous lullaby. Maybe she was still hoping that he would borrow money to buy rice. Unconsciously, hot tears streamed down his face. Seeing his expression, Hemp-faced A San said, "Okay! Let's see how many meals you can skip. It's no use crying a river!" Xiao Chen added, "People who come in here for the first time are all anxious and can't eat anything. Let him sleep for a while."

He shook his head, indicating that he didn't want to sleep either, and asked Xiao Chen, "Is there a way to send a letter out?"

"It depends on the opportunity. If someone is released, you can ask them to take the letter. Otherwise, it will cost five yuan to ask the little sweeper to find a way to send it."

He was silent after hearing these words. He looked up at the wall, which was covered with many poems and couplets, and there was also a mimeographed declaration of someone, which was smeared with bedbug blood and could not be seen clearly. After they finished eating, they all sat together. Hemp-faced A San shouted, "Old Yu! Come and listen to the old comrade tell a story!" But he just nodded and still didn't come over to sit down. This so-called old comrade was about forty years old, with deep wrinkles on his forehead. At a glance, you could tell that he was a person who had experienced a lot of hardships. They forced this so-called old comrade to tell about his so-called underground life in recent years, but after he told it, he always had to add a little sentimental words. Hemp-faced A San was an illiterate boatman. After listening to the things the so-called old comrade told, he liked to raise one or two questions and discuss them with others. When he was happy, he was triumphant and noisy, until the person with a gun outside the door shouted, "Keep quiet!" Only then did he stop.

This room, which was less than one square zhang, had to sleep more than twenty people, so of course they were arranged horizontally and vertically, squeezed so tightly that their bones rattled. If someone got up in the middle of the night to urinate, it was impossible to squeeze back down after getting up. On his first night here, his heart ached, and he couldn't sleep at all. He lay in the corner, pulling a dirty, black corner of the quilt to cover his lower body, and fell into a hazy sleep around dawn. When the sound of the plane buzzed over the roof, Xiao Chen woke him up:

"Old Yu, it's eight o'clock. It's almost roll call. Get up!"

So he got up and sat down. Unexpectedly, he saw a four or five-year-old child in Room No. 4 across the way, seeing others eating fried dough sticks, and asking his father to buy him fried dough sticks too. He thought of his own eldest child at home again, who followed him to make hot water every morning and insisted on buying a fried dough stick or a crab shell. He didn't know what was going on today. Thinking of this, tears almost came out again.

After the roll call, many people were called away one after another. Some came back with tears in their eyes and moaning in their mouths, which was undoubtedly a result of being tortured. Sometimes men and women were lined up in a team and went out, and came back still lined up, which meant they were taking pictures and getting fingerprints. Sometimes men and women were lined up in a team and walked out with two ropes on both sides to block them, which meant they were being transferred to another agency. He stared at these people coming and going, lost in thought, until it was time for dinner, and Xiao Chen gave him a salted egg, and he ate a bowl of rice.

After finishing dinner, Hemp-faced A San stood alone inside the crack of the prison door, his eyes constantly looking out. In a moment, he danced and shouted, "Oh, here she comes! My dear, she's even prettier today!" At this time, the eyes of everyone in the room were focused outside the prison door. It turned out that every evening, this short-haired, slender girl of only eighteen or nineteen would come to each room to empty the chamber pots. When she unlocked the prison door and came inside, everyone became playful and smiling, and the room was filled with sounds of "Sister, I love you" and "My dear, why are you only here now?" It was as if all the sorrowful scenes of the earth had been transformed into a magnificent and colorful landscape by a spring breeze.

Science Talk

Is the Chicken Born from the Egg, or the Egg from the Chicken? 287

— From Mu

When the question "Is the chicken born from the egg, or the egg from the chicken?" is raised, the so-called celebrities and scholars shake their heads and say, "This is a very mysterious question that can never be solved." In fact, the question itself is not mysterious; what is mysterious is the minds of these celebrities and scholars. Under their mysterious minds, it's chicken lays egg, egg lays chicken, egg lays chicken, chicken lays egg; as for who comes first, only heaven knows.

Everyone knows that a chicken is a living organism, and an egg is the embryo of that organism. According to biology, an embryo is formed and produced by an already existing organism. Therefore, our answer to the question is: the chicken lays the egg.

However, this is still a formal understanding; moreover, if one answers only formally in this way, it also carries a mysterious color. Because if one only says "chicken lays egg" without discussing the origin of the chicken, it is very easy for people to say in return "egg lays chicken," otherwise where did the chicken come from? Was it created by God? Mysterious!

Darwin tells us that all existing organisms have gradually evolved from a small life that appeared in the process of the formation of the universe. A chicken is a living organism, and its formation process certainly cannot violate the iron law of biological evolution; it is absolutely not created by God. According to general common sense, a chicken is a domestic fowl, and its predecessor must have been a wild bird, which gradually became tame after long-term domestication by humans. Due to the relationship of "use it or lose it," its wings gradually lost their flying function, and thus gradually formed the current shape of the chicken. As for this wild bird that formed the chicken, it was of course also evolved from a small organism that formed in the very beginning. Therefore, fundamentally speaking, the chicken is evolved from a certain organism that appeared in the formation process of the universe.

An egg is the embryo of an already existing chicken, or more precisely, it is the embryo of a chicken that has evolved along with the evolution of all living organisms. In this sense, only in this consciousness can we say that the already existing chicken comes first, and then the egg, as the embryo of the chicken, comes later; it is the chicken that lays the egg, not the egg that lays the chicken.

Here, some people may ask: the so-called wild bird, the predecessor of the chicken, must also be laid by an egg. Then, can't we say that the chicken is laid by an egg? This is easy to answer. First, the egg that produces the wild bird, the predecessor of the chicken, is not a chicken egg; second, as mentioned above, there must first be an organism, and then there will be the embryo of the organism. Similarly, there must first be a wild bird, and then there will be the egg of the wild bird as its embryo. Therefore, even for wild birds, there must first be the body, and then the egg as its embryo; thus, third, there is still the chicken first, and then the egg. If we still want to pursue the ultimate, to trace the origin of primitive organisms from the relationship between chicken and egg, and the relationship between wild bird and wild bird egg, then we can only attribute it to the matter in motion. In this way, the problem is not only not mysterious at all, but can also be solved scientifically.

Outlying Postal Agency

The Emperor's Cook and the Ming Dynasty's Soup 288

— Pei Lixia

Beiping Correspondence　　Anyone who has lived in Beiping for a few years will always have a deep impression of this gray ancient capital in their minds. Because, people here can not only see a peaceful and tranquil living environment; at the same time, because Beiping is a historically ancient capital, people here can also understand the remnants of past China and past Eastern culture from the environment!

In recent decades, although Western civilization has been constantly impacting this ancient city, we can still find traces of ancient culture everywhere in this declining city.

For example, the majestic imperial palace, the beautiful gardens, the imperial river with lotus flowers blooming in May, and the solemn ancestral temple with pine and cypress trees—which of these would not give people a deep impression? Which of these would not make people trace the past of China? ｜｜｜Not only these, but even in some small aspects of diet and daily life, it is the same.

If you don't believe it, I can give you some simple facts. For example, in terms of diet.

Many restaurants in Beiping often have a very long history, among which the most famous are Dongxinglou and Shaguoju.

Dongxinglou is located on the north side of Dong'anmen Street in the east of the city. It is said that it has been open since the Qing Dynasty and has been around for hundreds of years. The exterior of this restaurant is very old, with low bungalows and a gray-black surface. The architecture is naturally in the old style of hundreds of years ago. The light is not good, and the air is not circulating. All the furnishings inside are some mahogany square tables, flat beds, and chairs and stools. It is said that the cooks here are former imperial cooks, and the current chef is the one who used to cook for Xuantong. Because of this relationship, Dongxinglou has become a place for many dignitaries to entertain guests. In front of this old building, there are often many cars parked, and the dishes here are also particularly expensive. It is said that the price of an imperial cook is also particularly high. It is said that an imperial cook here only fries one dish, "Snowflake Chicken Stir-Fry," every day, but his monthly salary is more than one hundred yuan. Naturally, his rewards can be imagined.

In addition, there is also a Shaguoju. This is a bit more civilian-friendly. This place only sells pork and things from inside the pig's belly. There are not many dishes, but they are very famous. The reason for its fame is not because of the dishes, but mainly because of its history. It is said that this restaurant has been open since the Ming Dynasty. The casserole for stewing soup inside has been passed down from the Ming Dynasty. Since the Ming Dynasty, because water has been constantly added to this casserole, it has never dried out. Therefore, if you go to eat its soup now, you can still taste the soup inherited from the Ming Dynasty, perhaps eating one ten-thousandth of one ten-thousandth of the soup from the Ming Dynasty. At the same time, the rice they cook is the rice from the former imperial fields. Because of this historical legend, many people always flock to this Shaguoju. During Zhang Zongchang's heyday, he even held a grand banquet here for his guests.

A long time ago, I was also moved by this interesting legend and went with two friends to visit this "Ming Dynasty Soup" on Xisi North Street. We searched for a long time and finally found this place. This place is extremely low, with two or three bungalows, and the height is at most a little over ten feet. At the entrance, there is a signboard that has rotted to the point where it cannot be recognized. Inside, there are two small signboards that read: "Kyoto First" and "No Branches." We walked in and occupied a white wooden square table in a very narrow room. In addition to the characteristics of poor light and poor air circulation, there is also the fact that all the waiters are old men in their sixties and seventies. As soon as you call him, he always bends over and slowly deals with you.

It was here that we ate the rice that the emperor used to eat and also drank the so-called "Ming Dynasty Soup"｜Especially throwing us back to a place hundreds of years ago for a revisit.

No matter how fast the times are moving, Beiping still retains remnants of ancient Eastern culture in all aspects. Here, there are not only trams and cars, but also the emperor's cook and the Ming Dynasty's soup. These do not need to be collected by historical museums; they are naturally displayed there.

Book and Newspaper Introduction

How to Study the Current Monetary Problem? 289

— Jianfu

｜Introduction to Several Introductory Books｜

Recently, due to the US inflation, buying gold, raising silver prices, and other things, many studious young people have been dazzled and don't know where to start. Reading newspapers can only let you know a little bit of the facts, and reading magazines and buying books can't find an introductory path that is suitable for your appetite and digestible. Regarding this, not only are many of our amateur young people unable to figure it out, but even many college students and college graduates are not very clear. A few days ago, someone wrote a letter to Shenbao's "Reading Q&A" column asking for reading guidance, but the result of the reading guidance was only about introductory books on general economic theory; for the current urgent monetary problem to be solved, only Hilferding's "Financial Capital" was introduced. I think this is definitely not enough, not to mention that "Financial Capital" is a very difficult and specialized book.

Then how can we solve this problem?｜This is indeed not something that can be done in a few words. Instead of talking about it at length here, I think it would be simpler to introduce several easy-to-understand books to readers.

First of all, it must be stated that there are very few books in Chinese that are easy to understand and systematic. If readers have more free time, they can buy Zhu Binyuan's "Monetary Banking" to read, and it would be even better to buy Takahashi Yoshiki's "Practical Economics" translated by Shi Zhouhe to read (mainly reading the second part). If you don't have much free time, then buy a copy of the "Economic Common Sense" in the Wanyou Library to read, which is always helpful.

Although the above books can be used as a reference for beginners, they are inevitably subject to considerable distortions in theory. However, for the sake of friends who are eager to understand the current monetary phenomenon, this is also the best way to do it.

In English, although there are many textbooks and monographs on monetary issues, it is very difficult to gain insight into the current international monetary issues in the shortest possible time. Fortunately, several very easy-to-understand books have been published recently, and readers may wish to read them.

In the past year, as a result of the implementation of US monetary policy, not only experts and scholars have been arguing, but also the general American public has paid great attention to this issue. In order to meet the needs of the general public, many popular monetary arrangement theory books have emerged. Now, I will introduce four of the more complete books that have already arrived in Shanghai:

(1) "DollarsandSenseOuesrionsandAnswersinFinance"byBrant'

R｜｜This book is compiled in the form of questions and answers. There are clear explanations of general issues and theories of currency, finance, and even finance. Reading this book, you can get a general understanding of the monetary problems that are raging internationally.

(2) "ThePrimeroffnflationbySparlingE||This book is a very easy-to-understand book about "inflation." The "buying gold," "devaluing the gold standard," "raising silver prices," and so on that we see in newspapers and magazines, although there are many tricks, are nothing more than branches of currency expansion. By understanding the essence of inflation, these side branches can naturally be solved easily.

(3) "Tnflation",bywoodwqrd＆Ｒose｜｜To the extent of being popular, the above is "currency stability." After reading their reasons for opposing inflation, we can better understand the true picture of the currency issue. This book also has a very complete description of the history of past monetary expansion and monetary contraction.　(4) "SilvoriAnAoalysisofFactorsAffectingLt'sprice",byLeong,YＳ．｜｜Isn't the silver price issue raging recently? So, if you want to understand the past and current silver issues, silver price issues, etc., this book is worth reading.

Of the above four types, the first three are priced at US$1.10 each, and the last one is US$2. Converted to national currency, the former is less than 5 yuan, and the latter is about 6.5 yuan. The price is indeed a bit expensive. It is best for several people to pool their money to buy one, or ask a nearby library to subscribe.

Finally, let me add a sentence: American books are finally American books. The main purpose of the first few authors is almost to consider the business and property of the readers. Therefore, although these books can help us to understand the phenomenon, they are not necessarily the most correct theoretical books. If you have time, readers should buy a copy of E. Beros’ “TbeOnlyWayOdt” to read. In contrast, what you get is the only "Lu Gao Zhuang" (a famous Chinese sauce braised pork dish).
